00414 integer(I4P), parameter:: maxlen  = 500      !< Max number of characters of static string.
00415 character(1), parameter:: end_rec = char(10) !< End-character for binary-record finalize.
00416 integer(I4P), parameter:: ascii   = 0        !< Ascii-output-format parameter identifier.
00417 integer(I4P), parameter:: binary  = 1        !< Base64-output-format parameter identifier.
00418 integer(I4P), parameter:: raw     = 2        !< Raw-appended-binary-output-format parameter identifier.
00419 integer(I4P), parameter:: bin_app = 3        !< Base64-appended-output-format parameter identifier.
00420 ! VTK file data:
00421 type:: Type_VTK_File
00422   integer(I4P)::          f        = ascii !< Current output-format (initialized to ascii format).
00423   character(len=maxlen):: topology = ''    !< Mesh topology.
00424   integer(I4P)::          u        = 0_I4P !< Logical unit.
00425   integer(I4P)::          ua       = 0_I4P !< Logical unit for raw binary XML append file.
00426 #ifdef HUGE
00427   integer(I8P)::          N_Byte   = 0_I8P !< Number of byte to be written/read.
00428 #else
00429   integer(I4P)::          N_Byte   = 0_I4P !< Number of byte to be written/read.
00430 #endif
00431   integer(I8P)::          ioffset  = 0_I8P !< Offset pointer.
00432   integer(I4P)::          indent   = 0_I4P !< Indent pointer.
00433   contains
00434     procedure, non_overridable:: byte_update ! Procedure for updating N_Byte and ioffset pointer.
00435 endtype Type_VTK_File
00436 type(Type_VTK_File), allocatable:: vtk(:)       !< Global data of VTK files [1:Nvtk].
00437 integer(I4P)::                     Nvtk = 0_I4P !< Number of (concurrent) VTK files.
00438 integer(I4P)::                     f    = 0_I4P !< Current VTK file index.
00439 ! VTM file data:
00440 type:: Type_VTM_File
00441   integer(I4P):: u      = 0_I4P !< Logical unit.
00442   integer(I4P):: blk    = 0_I4P !< Block index.
00443   integer(I4P):: indent = 0_I4P !< Indent pointer.
00444 endtype Type_VTM_File
00445 type(Type_VTM_File):: vtm !< Global data of VTM files.

00449   ! The library uses five auxiliary procedures that are private thus they cannot be called outside the library.
00456   integer function Get_Unit(Free_Unit)
00457   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00458   implicit none
00459   integer, intent(OUT), optional:: Free_Unit !< Free logic unit.
00460   integer::                        n1        !< Counter.
00461   integer::                        ios       !< Inquiring flag.
00462   logical::                        lopen     !< Inquiring flag.
00463   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00464 
00465   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00466   Get_Unit = -1
00467   n1=1
00468   do
00469     if ((n1/=stdout).AND.(n1/=stderr)) then
00470       inquire(unit=n1,opened=lopen,iostat=ios)
00471       if (ios==0) then
00472         if (.NOT.lopen) then
00473           Get_Unit = n1 ; if (present(Free_Unit)) Free_Unit = Get_Unit
00474           return
00475         endif
00476       endif
00477     endif
00478     n1=n1+1
00479   enddo
00480   return
00481   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00482   endfunction Get_Unit

00490   elemental function Upper_Case(string)
00491   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00492   implicit none
00493   character(len=*), intent(IN):: string     !< String to be converted.
00494   character(len=len(string))::   Upper_Case !< Converted string.
00495   integer::                      n1         !< Characters counter.
00496   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00497 
00498   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00499   Upper_Case = string
00500   do n1=1,len(string)
00501     select case(ichar(string(n1:n1)))
00502     case(97:122)
00503       Upper_Case(n1:n1)=char(ichar(string(n1:n1))-32) ! Upper case conversion
00504     endselect
00505   enddo
00506   return
00507   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00508   endfunction Upper_Case

00511   elemental subroutine byte_update(vtk,N_Byte)
00512   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00513   implicit none
00514   class(Type_VTK_File), intent(INOUT):: vtk    !< Global data of VTK file.
00515 #ifdef HUGE
00516   integer(I8P),         intent(IN)::    N_Byte !< Number of bytes saved.
00517 #else
00518   integer(I4P),         intent(IN)::    N_Byte !< Number of bytes saved.
00519 #endif
00520   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00521 
00522   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00523   vtk%N_Byte = N_Byte
00524   if (vtk%f==raw) then
00525 #ifdef HUGE
00526     vtk%ioffset = vtk%ioffset + BYI8P + N_Byte
00527 #else
00528     vtk%ioffset = vtk%ioffset + BYI4P + N_Byte
00529 #endif
00530   else
00531 #ifdef HUGE
00532     vtk%ioffset = vtk%ioffset + ((N_Byte + BYI8P + 2_I8P)/3_I8P)*4_I8P
00533 #else
00534     vtk%ioffset = vtk%ioffset + ((N_Byte + BYI4P + 2_I4P)/3_I4P)*4_I4P
00535 #endif
00536   endif
00537   return
00538   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00539   endsubroutine byte_update
00540 
00542   pure subroutine vtk_update(act,cf,Nvtk,vtk)
00543   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00544   implicit none
00545   character(*),                     intent(IN)::    act        !< Action: 'ADD' one more element, 'REMOVE' current element file.
00546   integer(I4P),                     intent(INOUT):: cf         !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
00547   integer(I4P),                     intent(INOUT):: Nvtk       !< Number of (concurrent) VTK files.
00548   type(Type_VTK_File), allocatable, intent(INOUT):: vtk(:)     !< VTK files data.
00549   type(Type_VTK_File), allocatable::                vtk_tmp(:) !< Temporary array of VTK files data.
00550   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00551 
00552   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00553   select case(Upper_Case(trim(act)))
00554   case('ADD')
00555     if (Nvtk>0_I4P) then
00556       allocate(vtk_tmp(1:Nvtk))
00557       vtk_tmp = vtk
00558       deallocate(vtk)
00559       Nvtk = Nvtk + 1
00560       allocate(vtk(1:Nvtk))
00561       vtk(1:Nvtk-1) = vtk_tmp
00562       deallocate(vtk_tmp)
00563       cf = Nvtk
00564     else
00565       Nvtk = 1_I4P
00566       allocate(vtk(1:Nvtk))
00567       cf = Nvtk
00568     endif
00569   case default
00570     if (Nvtk>1_I4P) then
00571       allocate(vtk_tmp(1:Nvtk-1))
00572       if (cf==Nvtk) then
00573         vtk_tmp = vtk(1:Nvtk-1)
00574       else
00575         vtk_tmp(1 :cf-1) = vtk(1   :cf-1)
00576         vtk_tmp(cf:    ) = vtk(cf+1:    )
00577       endif
00578       deallocate(vtk)
00579       Nvtk = Nvtk - 1
00580       allocate(vtk(1:Nvtk))
00581       vtk = vtk_tmp
00582       deallocate(vtk_tmp)
00583       cf = 1_I4P
00584     else
00585       Nvtk = 0_I4P
00586       if (allocated(vtk)) deallocate(vtk)
00587       cf = Nvtk
00588     endif
00589   endselect
00590   return
00591   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00592   endsubroutine vtk_update

00596   pure function tochar(string) result (char_string)
00597   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00598   implicit none
00599   character(1), intent(IN)::      string(1:)  !< Array of 1 character.
00600   character(size(string,dim=1)):: char_string !< String of characters.
00601   integer(I4P)::                  i           !< Counter.
00602   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00603 
00604   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00605   forall(i = 1:size(string,dim=1))
00606      char_string(i:i) = string(i)
00607   endforall
00608   return
00609   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00610   endfunction tochar

00638   function VTK_INI_XML(output_format,filename,mesh_topology,cf,nx1,nx2,ny1,ny2,nz1,nz2) result(E_IO)
00639   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00640   implicit none
00641   character(*), intent(IN)::            output_format !< Output format: ASCII, BINARY, RAW or BINARY-APPENDED.
00642   character(*), intent(IN)::            filename      !< File name.
00643   character(*), intent(IN)::            mesh_topology !< Mesh topology.
00644   integer(I4P), intent(OUT), optional:: cf            !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
00645   integer(I4P), intent(IN),  optional:: nx1           !< Initial node of x axis.
00646   integer(I4P), intent(IN),  optional:: nx2           !< Final node of x axis.
00647   integer(I4P), intent(IN),  optional:: ny1           !< Initial node of y axis.
00648   integer(I4P), intent(IN),  optional:: ny2           !< Final node of y axis.
00649   integer(I4P), intent(IN),  optional:: nz1           !< Initial node of z axis.
00650   integer(I4P), intent(IN),  optional:: nz2           !< Final node of z axis.
00651   integer(I4P)::                        E_IO          !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
00652   character(len=maxlen)::               s_buffer      !< Buffer string.
00653   integer(I4P)::                        rf            !< Real file index.
00654   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00655 
00656   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00657   E_IO = -1_I4P
00658   if (.not.ir_initialized) call IR_Init
00659   call vtk_update(act='add',cf=rf,Nvtk=Nvtk,vtk=vtk)
00660   f = rf
00661   if (present(cf)) cf = rf
00662   vtk(rf)%topology = trim(mesh_topology)
00663   select case(trim(Upper_Case(output_format)))
00664   case('ASCII')
00665     vtk(rf)%f = ascii
00666     open(unit=Get_Unit(vtk(rf)%u),file=trim(filename),form='FORMATTED',&
00667          access='SEQUENTIAL',action='WRITE',status='REPLACE',iostat=E_IO)
00668     ! writing header of file
00669     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)'<?xml version="1.0"?>'
00670     if (endian==endianL) then
00671       s_buffer = '<VTKFile type="'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//'" version="0.1" byte_order="LittleEndian">'
00672     else
00673       s_buffer = '<VTKFile type="'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//'" version="0.1" byte_order="BigEndian">'
00674     endif
00675     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtk(rf)%indent = 2
00676     select case(trim(vtk(rf)%topology))
00677     case('RectilinearGrid','StructuredGrid')
00678       s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//' WholeExtent="'//&
00679                  trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '//                             &
00680                  trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '//                             &
00681                  trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
00682     case('UnstructuredGrid')
00683       s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//'>'
00684     endselect
00685     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
00686   case('RAW','BINARY-APPENDED')
00687     vtk(rf)%f = raw
00688     if (trim(Upper_Case(output_format))=='BINARY-APPENDED') vtk(rf)%f = bin_app
00689     open(unit=Get_Unit(vtk(rf)%u),file=trim(filename),&
00690          form='UNFORMATTED',access='STREAM',action='WRITE',status='REPLACE',iostat=E_IO)
00691     ! writing header of file
00692     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'<?xml version="1.0"?>'//end_rec
00693     if (endian==endianL) then
00694       s_buffer = '<VTKFile type="'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//'" version="0.1" byte_order="LittleEndian">'
00695     else
00696       s_buffer = '<VTKFile type="'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//'" version="0.1" byte_order="BigEndian">'
00697     endif
00698     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = 2
00699     select case(trim(vtk(rf)%topology))
00700     case('RectilinearGrid','StructuredGrid')
00701       s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//' WholeExtent="'//&
00702                  trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '//                             &
00703                  trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '//                             &
00704                  trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
00705     case('UnstructuredGrid')
00706       s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//'>'
00707     endselect
00708     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
00709     ! opening the SCRATCH file used for appending raw binary data
00710     open(unit=Get_Unit(vtk(rf)%ua), form='UNFORMATTED', access='STREAM', action='READWRITE', status='SCRATCH', iostat=E_IO)
00711     vtk(rf)%ioffset = 0 ! initializing offset pointer
00712   case('BINARY')
00713     vtk(rf)%f = binary
00714     open(unit=Get_Unit(vtk(rf)%u),file=trim(filename),&
00715          form='UNFORMATTED',access='STREAM',action='WRITE',status='REPLACE',iostat=E_IO)
00716     ! writing header of file
00717     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'<?xml version="1.0"?>'//end_rec
00718     if (endian==endianL) then
00719       s_buffer = '<VTKFile type="'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//'" version="0.1" byte_order="LittleEndian">'
00720     else
00721       s_buffer = '<VTKFile type="'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//'" version="0.1" byte_order="BigEndian">'
00722     endif
00723     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = 2
00724     select case(trim(vtk(rf)%topology))
00725     case('RectilinearGrid','StructuredGrid')
00726       s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//' WholeExtent="'//&
00727                  trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '//                             &
00728                  trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '//                             &
00729                  trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
00730     case('UnstructuredGrid')
00731       s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//'>'
00732     endselect
00733     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
00734   endselect
00735   return
00736   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00737   endfunction VTK_INI_XML
00738 
00743   function VTK_FLD_XML_OC(fld_action,cf) result(E_IO)
00744   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00745   implicit none
00746   character(*), intent(IN)::           fld_action !< Field data tag action: OPEN or CLOSE tag.
00747   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf         !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
00748   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO       !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
00749   integer(I4P)::                       rf         !< Real file index.
00750   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00751 
00752   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00753   E_IO = -1_I4P
00754   rf = f
00755   if (present(cf)) then
00756     rf = cf ; f = cf
00757   endif
00758   select case(trim(Upper_Case(fld_action)))
00759   case('OPEN')
00760     select case(vtk(rf)%f)
00761     case(ascii)
00762       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<FieldData>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
00763     case(raw,binary,bin_app)
00764       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<FieldData>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
00765     endselect
00766   case('CLOSE')
00767     select case(vtk(rf)%f)
00768     case(ascii)
00769       vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</FieldData>'
00770     case(raw,binary,bin_app)
00771       vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</FieldData>'//end_rec
00772     endselect
00773   endselect
00774   return
00775   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
00776   endfunction VTK_FLD_XML_OC

00802              trim(str(n=fld))//'</DataArray>'

00923   integer(I1P), allocatable::          fldp(:)  !< Packed field data.

00937                trim(str(n=fld))//'</DataArray>'
00938     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
00939   case(raw,bin_app)
00940     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int32" NumberOfTuples="1" Name="'//trim(fname)// &

01047 
01050   function VTK_GEO_XML_STRG_1DA_R8(nx1,nx2,ny1,ny2,nz1,nz2,NN,X,Y,Z,cf) result(E_IO)
01051   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01052   implicit none
01053   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nx1      !< Initial node of x axis.
01054   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nx2      !< Final node of x axis.
01055   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           ny1      !< Initial node of y axis.
01056   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           ny2      !< Final node of y axis.
01057   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nz1      !< Initial node of z axis.
01058   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nz2      !< Final node of z axis.
01059   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NN       !< Number of all nodes.
01060   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           X(1:)    !< X coordinates [1:NN].
01061   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           Y(1:)    !< Y coordinates [1:NN].
01062   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           Z(1:)    !< Z coordinates [1:NN].
01063   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf       !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
01064   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO     !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
01065   integer(I1P), allocatable::          XYZp(:)  !< Packed coordinates data.
01066   character(1), allocatable::          XYZ64(:) !< X, Y, Z coordinates encoded in base64.
01067   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer !< Buffer string.
01068   integer(I4P)::                       rf       !< Real file index.
01069   integer(I4P)::                       n1       !< Counter.
01070   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01071 
01072   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01073   E_IO = -1_I4P
01074   rf = f
01075   if (present(cf)) then
01076     rf = cf ; f = cf
01077   endif
01078   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
01079   case(ascii)
01080     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01081                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01082                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01083     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01084     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01085     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="ascii">'
01086     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
01087     do n1=1,NN
01088       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//str(n=X(n1))//' '//str(n=Y(n1))//' '//str(n=Z(n1))
01089     enddo
01090     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
01091     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'
01092   case(raw,bin_app)
01093     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01094                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01095                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01096     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01097     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01098     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//                                                                  &
01099                '<DataArray type="Float64" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="appended" offset="'// &
01100                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
01101     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01102     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = 3*NN*BYR8P)
01103     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'R8',3*NN
01104     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(X(n1),Y(n1),Z(n1),n1=1,NN)
01105     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'//end_rec
01106   case(binary)
01107     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01108                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01109                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01110     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01111     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01112     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="binary">'
01113     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01114     call pack_data(a1=[int(3*NN*BYR8P,I4P)],a2=[(X(n1),Y(n1),Z(n1),n1=1,NN)],packed=XYZp)
01115     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=XYZp,code=XYZ64) ; deallocate(XYZp)
01116     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(XYZ64)//end_rec ; deallocate(XYZ64)
01117     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
01118     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'//end_rec
01119   endselect
01120   return
01121   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01122   endfunction VTK_GEO_XML_STRG_1DA_R8
01123 
01126   function VTK_GEO_XML_STRG_3DA_R8(nx1,nx2,ny1,ny2,nz1,nz2,NN,X,Y,Z,cf) result(E_IO)
01127   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01128   implicit none
01129   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nx1               !< Initial node of x axis.
01130   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nx2               !< Final node of x axis.
01131   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           ny1               !< Initial node of y axis.
01132   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           ny2               !< Final node of y axis.
01133   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nz1               !< Initial node of z axis.
01134   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nz2               !< Final node of z axis.
01135   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NN                !< Number of all nodes.
01136   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           X(nx1:,ny1:,nz1:) !< X coordinates [nx1:nx2,ny1:ny2,nz1:nz2].
01137   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           Y(nx1:,ny1:,nz1:) !< Y coordinates [nx1:nx2,ny1:ny2,nz1:nz2].
01138   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           Z(nx1:,ny1:,nz1:) !< Z coordinates [nx1:nx2,ny1:ny2,nz1:nz2].
01139   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf                !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
01140   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO              !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
01141   integer(I1P), allocatable::          XYZp(:)           !< Packed coordinates data.
01142   character(1), allocatable::          XYZ64(:)          !< X, Y, Z coordinates encoded in base64.
01143   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer          !< Buffer string.
01144   integer(I4P)::                       rf                !< Real file index.
01145   integer(I4P)::                       nx,ny,nz          !< Counters.
01146   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01147 
01148   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01149   E_IO = -1_I4P
01150   rf = f
01151   if (present(cf)) then
01152     rf = cf ; f = cf
01153   endif
01154   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
01155   case(ascii)
01156     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01157                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01158                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01159     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01160     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01161     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="ascii">'
01162     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
01163     do nz=nz1,nz2
01164       do ny=ny1,ny2
01165         do nx=nx1,nx2
01166           write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//&
01167                                                      str(n=X(nx,ny,nz))//' '//str(n=Y(nx,ny,nz))//' '//str(n=Z(nx,ny,nz))
01168         enddo
01169       enddo
01170     enddo
01171     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
01172     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'
01173   case(raw,bin_app)
01174     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01175                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01176                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01177     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01178     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01179     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//                                                                  &
01180                '<DataArray type="Float64" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="appended" offset="'// &
01181                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
01182     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01183     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = 3*NN*BYR8P)
01184     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'R8',3*NN
01185     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(((X(nx,ny,nz),Y(nx,ny,nz),Z(nx,ny,nz),nx=nx1,nx2),ny=ny1,ny2),nz=nz1,nz2)
01186     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'//end_rec
01187   case(binary)
01188     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01189                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01190                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01191     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01192     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01193     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="binary">'
01194     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01195     call pack_data(a1=[int(3*NN*BYR8P,I4P)],a2=[(((X(nx,ny,nz),Y(nx,ny,nz),Z(nx,ny,nz),nx=nx1,nx2),ny=ny1,ny2),nz=nz1,nz2)],&
01196                    packed=XYZp)
01197     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=XYZp,code=XYZ64) ; deallocate(XYZp)
01198     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(XYZ64)//end_rec ; deallocate(XYZ64)
01199     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
01200     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'//end_rec
01201   endselect
01202   return
01203   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01204   endfunction VTK_GEO_XML_STRG_3DA_R8

01208   function VTK_GEO_XML_STRG_1DAP_R8(nx1,nx2,ny1,ny2,nz1,nz2,NN,XYZ,cf) result(E_IO)
01209   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01210   implicit none

01212   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nx2        !< Final node of x axis.

01214   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           ny2        !< Final node of y axis.
01215   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nz1        !< Initial node of z axis.
01216   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nz2        !< Final node of z axis.
01217   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NN         !< Number of all nodes.
01218   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           XYZ(1:,1:) !< X, Y, Z coordinates (packed API) [1:3,1:NN].
01219   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf         !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
01220   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO       !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
01221   integer(I1P), allocatable::          XYZp(:)    !< Packed coordinates data.
01222   character(1), allocatable::          XYZ64(:)   !< X, Y, Z coordinates encoded in base64.
01223   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer   !< Buffer string.
01224   integer(I4P)::                       rf         !< Real file index.
01225   integer(I4P)::                       n1         !< Counter.
01226   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01227 
01228   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01229   E_IO = -1_I4P
01230   rf = f
01231   if (present(cf)) then
01232     rf = cf ; f = cf
01233   endif
01234   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
01235   case(ascii)
01236     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01237                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01238                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01239     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01240     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01241     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="ascii">'
01242     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
01243     do n1=1,NN
01244       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//&
01245                                                  str(n=XYZ(1,n1))//' '//str(n=XYZ(2,n1))//' '//str(n=XYZ(3,n1))
01246     enddo
01247     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
01248     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'
01249   case(raw,bin_app)
01250     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01251                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01252                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01253     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01254     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01255     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//                                                                  &
01256                '<DataArray type="Float64" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="appended" offset="'// &
01257                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
01258     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01259     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = 3*NN*BYR8P)
01260     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'R8',3*NN
01261     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)XYZ
01262     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'//end_rec
01263   case(binary)
01264     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01265                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01266                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01267     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01268     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01269     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="binary">'
01270     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01271     call pack_data(a1=[int(3*NN*BYR8P,I4P)],a2=reshape(XYZ,[3*NN]),packed=XYZp)
01272     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=XYZp,code=XYZ64) ; deallocate(XYZp)
01273     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(XYZ64)//end_rec ; deallocate(XYZ64)
01274     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
01275     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'//end_rec
01276   endselect
01277   return

01283   function VTK_GEO_XML_STRG_3DAP_R8(nx1,nx2,ny1,ny2,nz1,nz2,NN,XYZ,cf) result(E_IO)
01284   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01285   implicit none
01286   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nx1                    !< Initial node of x axis.
01287   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nx2                    !< Final node of x axis.
01288   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           ny1                    !< Initial node of y axis.
01289   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           ny2                    !< Final node of y axis.
01290   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nz1                    !< Initial node of z axis.
01291   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nz2                    !< Final node of z axis.
01292   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NN                     !< Number of all nodes.
01293   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           XYZ(1:,nx1:,ny1:,nz1:) !< X, Y, Z coordinates (packed API).
01294   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf                     !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
01295   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO              !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
01296   integer(I1P), allocatable::          XYZp(:)                !< Packed coordinates data.
01297   character(1), allocatable::          XYZ64(:)               !< X, Y, Z coordinates encoded in base64.
01298   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer               !< Buffer string.
01299   integer(I4P)::                       rf                     !< Real file index.
01300   integer(I4P)::                       nx,ny,nz               !< Counters.
01301   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01302 
01303   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01304   E_IO = -1_I4P
01305   rf = f
01306   if (present(cf)) then
01307     rf = cf ; f = cf
01308   endif
01309   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
01310   case(ascii)
01311     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01312                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01313                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01314     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01315     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01316     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="ascii">'
01317     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
01318     do nz=nz1,nz2
01319       do ny=ny1,ny2
01320         do nx=nx1,nx2
01321           write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//&
01322                                                     str(n=XYZ(1,nx,ny,nz))//' '//str(n=XYZ(2,nx,ny,nz))//' '//str(n=XYZ(3,nx,ny,nz))
01323         enddo
01324       enddo
01325     enddo
01326     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
01327     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'
01328   case(raw,bin_app)
01329     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01330                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01331                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'

01333     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01334     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//                                                                  &
01335                '<DataArray type="Float64" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="appended" offset="'// &
01336                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
01337     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01338     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = 3*NN*BYR8P)
01339     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'R8',3*NN
01340     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)XYZ
01341     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'//end_rec
01342   case(binary)
01343     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01344                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01345                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01346     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01347     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2

01350     call pack_data(a1=[int(3*NN*BYR8P,I4P)],a2=reshape(XYZ,[3*NN]),packed=XYZp)
01351     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=XYZp,code=XYZ64) ; deallocate(XYZp)

01362   function VTK_GEO_XML_STRG_1DA_R4(nx1,nx2,ny1,ny2,nz1,nz2,NN,X,Y,Z,cf) result(E_IO)
01363   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01364   implicit none
01365   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nx1      !< Initial node of x axis.
01366   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nx2      !< Final node of x axis.
01367   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           ny1      !< Initial node of y axis.
01368   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           ny2      !< Final node of y axis.
01369   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nz1      !< Initial node of z axis.
01370   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nz2      !< Final node of z axis.
01371   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NN       !< Number of all nodes.
01372   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::           X(1:)    !< X coordinates [1:NN].
01373   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::           Y(1:)    !< Y coordinates [1:NN].
01374   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::           Z(1:)    !< Z coordinates [1:NN].
01375   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf       !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
01376   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO     !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
01377   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer !< Buffer string.
01378   integer(I1P), allocatable::          XYZp(:)  !< Packed data.
01379   character(1), allocatable::          XYZ64(:) !< X, Y, Z coordinates encoded in base64.
01380   integer(I4P)::                       rf       !< Real file index.
01381   integer(I4P)::                       n1       !< Counter.
01382   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01383 
01384   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01385   E_IO = -1_I4P
01386   rf = f
01387   if (present(cf)) then
01388     rf = cf ; f = cf
01389   endif
01390   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
01391   case(ascii)
01392     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01393                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01394                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01395     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01396     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01397     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float32" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="ascii">'
01398     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
01399     do n1=1,NN
01400       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//str(n=X(n1))//' '//str(n=Y(n1))//' '//str(n=Z(n1))
01401     enddo
01402     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
01403     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'
01404   case(raw,bin_app)
01405     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01406                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01407                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01408     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01409     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01410     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//                                                                  &
01411                '<DataArray type="Float32" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="appended" offset="'// &
01412                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
01413     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01414     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = 3*NN*BYR4P)
01415     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'R4',3*NN
01416     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(X(n1),Y(n1),Z(n1),n1=1,NN)
01417     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'//end_rec
01418   case(binary)
01419     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01420                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01421                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01422     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01423     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01424     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float32" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="binary">'
01425     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01426     call pack_data(a1=[int(3*NN*BYR4P,I4P)],a2=[(X(n1),Y(n1),Z(n1),n1=1,NN)],packed=XYZp)
01427     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=XYZp,code=XYZ64) ; deallocate(XYZp)
01428     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(XYZ64)//end_rec ; deallocate(XYZ64)
01429     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
01430     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'//end_rec
01431   endselect
01432   return
01433   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01434   endfunction VTK_GEO_XML_STRG_1DA_R4

01438   function VTK_GEO_XML_STRG_3DA_R4(nx1,nx2,ny1,ny2,nz1,nz2,NN,X,Y,Z,cf) result(E_IO)
01439   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01440   implicit none
01441   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nx1               !< Initial node of x axis.
01442   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nx2               !< Final node of x axis.
01443   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           ny1               !< Initial node of y axis.
01444   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           ny2               !< Final node of y axis.
01445   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nz1               !< Initial node of z axis.
01446   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nz2               !< Final node of z axis.
01447   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NN                !< Number of all nodes.
01448   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::           X(nx1:,ny1:,nz1:) !< X coordinates [nx1:nx2,ny1:ny2,nz1:nz2].
01449   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::           Y(nx1:,ny1:,nz1:) !< Y coordinates [nx1:nx2,ny1:ny2,nz1:nz2].
01450   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::           Z(nx1:,ny1:,nz1:) !< Z coordinates [nx1:nx2,ny1:ny2,nz1:nz2].
01451   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf                !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
01452   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO              !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
01453   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer          !< Buffer string.
01454   integer(I1P), allocatable::          XYZp(:)           !< Packed data.
01455   character(1), allocatable::          XYZ64(:)          !< X, Y, Z coordinates encoded in base64.
01456   integer(I4P)::                       rf                !< Real file index.
01457   integer(I4P)::                       nx,ny,nz          !< Counters.
01458   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01459 
01460   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01461   E_IO = -1_I4P
01462   rf = f
01463   if (present(cf)) then
01464     rf = cf ; f = cf
01465   endif
01466   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
01467   case(ascii)
01468     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01469                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01470                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01471     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01472     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01473     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float32" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="ascii">'
01474     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
01475     do nz=nz1,nz2
01476       do ny=ny1,ny2
01477         do nx=nx1,nx2
01478           write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//&
01479                                                      str(n=X(nx,ny,nz))//' '//str(n=Y(nx,ny,nz))//' '//str(n=Z(nx,ny,nz))
01480         enddo
01481       enddo
01482     enddo
01483     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
01484     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'
01485   case(raw,bin_app)
01486     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01487                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01488                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01489     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01490     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01491     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//                                                                  &
01492                '<DataArray type="Float32" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="appended" offset="'// &
01493                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
01494     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01495     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = 3*NN*BYR4P)
01496     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'R4',3*NN
01497     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(((X(nx,ny,nz),Y(nx,ny,nz),Z(nx,ny,nz),nx=nx1,nx2),ny=ny1,ny2),nz=nz1,nz2)
01498     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'//end_rec
01499   case(binary)
01500     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01501                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01502                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01503     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01504     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01505     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float32" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="binary">'
01506     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01507     call pack_data(a1=[int(3*NN*BYR4P,I4P)],a2=[(((X(nx,ny,nz),Y(nx,ny,nz),Z(nx,ny,nz),nx=nx1,nx2),ny=ny1,ny2),nz=nz1,nz2)], &
01508                    packed=XYZp)
01509     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=XYZp,code=XYZ64) ; deallocate(XYZp)
01510     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(XYZ64)//end_rec ; deallocate(XYZ64)
01511     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
01512     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'//end_rec
01513   endselect
01514   return
01515   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01516   endfunction VTK_GEO_XML_STRG_3DA_R4

01520   function VTK_GEO_XML_STRG_1DAP_R4(nx1,nx2,ny1,ny2,nz1,nz2,NN,XYZ,cf) result(E_IO)
01521   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01522   implicit none
01523   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nx1        !< Initial node of x axis.
01524   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nx2        !< Final node of x axis.
01525   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           ny1        !< Initial node of y axis.
01526   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           ny2        !< Final node of y axis.
01527   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nz1        !< Initial node of z axis.
01528   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nz2        !< Final node of z axis.
01529   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NN         !< Number of all nodes.
01530   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::           XYZ(1:,1:) !< X, Y, Z coordinates (packed API) [1:3,1:NN].
01531   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf         !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
01532   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO       !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
01533   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer   !< Buffer string.
01534   integer(I1P), allocatable::          XYZp(:)    !< Packed data.
01535   character(1), allocatable::          XYZ64(:)   !< X, Y, Z coordinates encoded in base64.
01536   integer(I4P)::                       rf         !< Real file index.
01537   integer(I4P)::                       n1         !< Counter.
01538   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01539 
01540   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01541   E_IO = -1_I4P
01542   rf = f
01543   if (present(cf)) then
01544     rf = cf ; f = cf
01545   endif
01546   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
01547   case(ascii)
01548     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01549                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01550                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01551     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01552     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01553     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float32" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="ascii">'
01554     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
01555     do n1=1,NN
01556       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//&
01557                                                  str(n=XYZ(1,n1))//' '//str(n=XYZ(2,n1))//' '//str(n=XYZ(3,n1))
01558     enddo
01559     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
01560     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'
01561   case(raw,bin_app)
01562     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01563                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01564                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01565     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01566     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01567     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//                                                                  &
01568                '<DataArray type="Float32" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="appended" offset="'// &
01569                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
01570     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01571     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = 3*NN*BYR4P)
01572     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'R4',3*NN
01573     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)XYZ
01574     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'//end_rec
01575   case(binary)
01576     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01577                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01578                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01579     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01580     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01581     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float32" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="binary">'
01582     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01583     call pack_data(a1=[int(3*NN*BYR4P,I4P)],a2=reshape(XYZ,[3*NN]),packed=XYZp)
01584     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=XYZp,code=XYZ64) ; deallocate(XYZp)
01585     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(XYZ64)//end_rec ; deallocate(XYZ64)
01586     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
01587     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'//end_rec
01588   endselect
01589   return
01590   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01591   endfunction VTK_GEO_XML_STRG_1DAP_R4
