01595   function VTK_GEO_XML_STRG_3DAP_R4(nx1,nx2,ny1,ny2,nz1,nz2,NN,XYZ,cf) result(E_IO)
01596   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01597   implicit none
01598   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nx1                    !< Initial node of x axis.
01599   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nx2                    !< Final node of x axis.
01600   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           ny1                    !< Initial node of y axis.
01601   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           ny2                    !< Final node of y axis.
01602   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nz1                    !< Initial node of z axis.
01603   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           nz2                    !< Final node of z axis.
01604   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NN                     !< Number of all nodes.
01605   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::           XYZ(1:,nx1:,ny1:,nz1:) !< X, Y, Z coordinates (packed API) [1:3,nx1:nx2,ny1:ny2,nz1:nz2].
01606   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf                     !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
01607   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO             !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
01608   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer               !< Buffer string.
01609   integer(I1P), allocatable::          XYZp(:)                !< Packed data.
01610   character(1), allocatable::          XYZ64(:)               !< X, Y, Z coordinates encoded in base64.
01611   integer(I4P)::                       rf                     !< Real file index.
01612   integer(I4P)::                       nx,ny,nz               !< Counters.
01613   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01614 
01615   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01616   E_IO = -1_I4P
01617   rf = f
01618   if (present(cf)) then
01619     rf = cf ; f = cf
01620   endif
01621   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
01622   case(ascii)
01623     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01624                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01625                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01626     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01627     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01628     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float32" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="ascii">'
01629     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
01630     do nz=nz1,nz2
01631       do ny=ny1,ny2
01632         do nx=nx1,nx2
01633           write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//&
01634                                                     str(n=XYZ(1,nx,ny,nz))//' '//str(n=XYZ(2,nx,ny,nz))//' '//str(n=XYZ(3,nx,ny,nz))
01635         enddo
01636       enddo
01637     enddo
01638     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
01639     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'
01640   case(raw,bin_app)
01641     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01642                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01643                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01644     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01645     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01646     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//                                                                  &
01647                '<DataArray type="Float32" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="appended" offset="'// &
01648                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
01649     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01650     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = 3*NN*BYR4P)
01651     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'R4',3*NN
01652     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)XYZ
01653     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'//end_rec
01654   case(binary)
01655     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01656                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01657                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01658     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01659     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01660     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float32" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="binary">'
01661     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01662     call pack_data(a1=[int(3*NN*BYR4P,I4P)],a2=reshape(XYZ,[3*NN]),packed=XYZp)
01663     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=XYZp,code=XYZ64) ; deallocate(XYZp)
01664     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(XYZ64)//end_rec ; deallocate(XYZ64)
01665     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
01666     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'//end_rec
01667   endselect
01668   return
01669   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01670   endfunction VTK_GEO_XML_STRG_3DAP_R4
01671 
01674   function VTK_GEO_XML_RECT_R8(nx1,nx2,ny1,ny2,nz1,nz2,X,Y,Z,cf) result(E_IO)
01675   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01676   implicit none
01677   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::             nx1        !< Initial node of x axis.
01678   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::             nx2        !< Final node of x axis.
01679   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::             ny1        !< Initial node of y axis.
01680   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::             ny2        !< Final node of y axis.
01681   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::             nz1        !< Initial node of z axis.
01682   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::             nz2        !< Final node of z axis.
01683   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::             X(nx1:nx2) !< X coordinates.
01684   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::             Y(ny1:ny2) !< Y coordinates.
01685   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::             Z(nz1:nz2) !< Z coordinates.
01686   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional::   cf         !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
01687   integer(I4P)::                         E_IO       !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
01688   character(len=maxlen)::                s_buffer   !< Buffer string.
01689   integer(I1P), allocatable::            XYZp(:)    !< Packed data.
01690   character(1), allocatable::            XYZ64(:)   !< X, Y, Z coordinates encoded in base64.
01691   integer(I4P)::                         rf         !< Real file index.
01692   integer(I4P)::                         n1         !< Counter.
01693   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01694 
01695   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01696   E_IO = -1_I4P
01697   rf = f
01698   if (present(cf)) then
01699     rf = cf ; f = cf
01700   endif
01701   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
01702   case(ascii)
01703     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01704                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01705                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01706     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01707     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Coordinates>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01708     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" Name="X" format="ascii">'
01709     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt=FR8P, iostat=E_IO)(X(n1),n1=nx1,nx2)
01710     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'
01711     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" Name="Y" format="ascii">'
01712     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt=FR8P, iostat=E_IO)(Y(n1),n1=ny1,ny2)
01713     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'
01714     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" Name="Z" format="ascii">'
01715     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt=FR8P, iostat=E_IO)(Z(n1),n1=nz1,nz2)
01716     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
01717     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Coordinates>'
01718   case(raw,bin_app)
01719     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01720                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01721                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01722     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01723     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Coordinates>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01724     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" Name="X" format="appended" offset="'//&
01725                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
01726     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01727     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = (nx2-nx1+1)*BYR8P)
01728     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'R8',(nx2-nx1+1)
01729     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(X(n1),n1=nx1,nx2)
01730     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" Name="Y" format="appended" offset="'//&
01731                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
01732     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01733     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = (ny2-ny1+1)*BYR8P)
01734     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'R8',(ny2-ny1+1)
01735     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(Y(n1),n1=ny1,ny2)
01736     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" Name="Z" format="appended" offset="'//&
01737                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
01738     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01739     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = (nz2-nz1+1)*BYR8P)
01740     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'R8',(nz2-nz1+1)
01741     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(Z(n1),n1=nz1,nz2)
01742     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Coordinates>'//end_rec
01743   case(binary)
01744     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01745                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01746                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01747     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01748     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Coordinates>'
01749     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01750     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" Name="X" format="binary">'
01751     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01752     call pack_data(a1=[int((nx2-nx1+1)*BYR8P,I4P)],a2=X,packed=XYZp)
01753     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=XYZp,code=XYZ64)
01754     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(XYZ64)//end_rec
01755     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
01756     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" Name="Y" format="binary">'
01757     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01758     call pack_data(a1=[int((ny2-ny1+1)*BYR8P,I4P)],a2=Y,packed=XYZp)
01759     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=XYZp,code=XYZ64)
01760     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(XYZ64)//end_rec
01761     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
01762     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" Name="Z" format="binary">'
01763     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01764     call pack_data(a1=[int((nz2-nz1+1)*BYR8P,I4P)],a2=Z,packed=XYZp)
01765     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=XYZp,code=XYZ64) ; deallocate(XYZp)
01766     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(XYZ64)//end_rec ; deallocate(XYZ64)
01767     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
01768     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
01769     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Coordinates>'//end_rec
01770   endselect
01771   return
01772   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01773   endfunction VTK_GEO_XML_RECT_R8
01774 
01777   function VTK_GEO_XML_RECT_R4(nx1,nx2,ny1,ny2,nz1,nz2,X,Y,Z,cf) result(E_IO)
01778   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01779   implicit none
01780   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::             nx1        !< Initial node of x axis.
01781   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::             nx2        !< Final node of x axis.
01782   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::             ny1        !< Initial node of y axis.
01783   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::             ny2        !< Final node of y axis.
01784   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::             nz1        !< Initial node of z axis.
01785   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::             nz2        !< Final node of z axis.
01786   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::             X(nx1:nx2) !< X coordinates.
01787   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::             Y(ny1:ny2) !< Y coordinates.
01788   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::             Z(nz1:nz2) !< Z coordinates.
01789   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional::   cf         !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
01790   integer(I4P)::                         E_IO       !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
01791   character(len=maxlen)::                s_buffer   !< Buffer string.
01792   integer(I1P), allocatable::            XYZp(:)    !< Packed data.
01793   character(1), allocatable::            XYZ64(:)   !< X, Y, Z coordinates encoded in base64.
01794   integer(I4P)::                         rf         !< Real file index.
01795   integer(I4P)::                         n1         !< Counter.
01796   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01797 
01798   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01799   E_IO = -1_I4P
01800   rf = f
01801   if (present(cf)) then
01802     rf = cf ; f = cf
01803   endif
01804   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
01805   case(ascii)
01806     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01807                                                       trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01808                                                       trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01809     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01810     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Coordinates>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01811     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float32" Name="X" format="ascii">'
01812     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt=FR4P, iostat=E_IO)(X(n1),n1=nx1,nx2)
01813     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'
01814     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float32" Name="Y" format="ascii">'
01815     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt=FR4P, iostat=E_IO)(Y(n1),n1=ny1,ny2)
01816     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'
01817     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float32" Name="Z" format="ascii">'
01818     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt=FR4P, iostat=E_IO)(Z(n1),n1=nz1,nz2)
01819     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
01820     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Coordinates>'
01821   case(raw,bin_app)
01822     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01823                                                       trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01824                                                       trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01825     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01826     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Coordinates>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01827     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float32" Name="X" format="appended" offset="'//&
01828                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
01829     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01830     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = (nx2-nx1+1)*BYR4P)
01831     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'R4',(nx2-nx1+1)
01832     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(X(n1),n1=nx1,nx2)
01833     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float32" Name="Y" format="appended" offset="'//&
01834                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
01835     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01836     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = (ny2-ny1+1)*BYR4P)
01837     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'R4',(ny2-ny1+1)
01838     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(Y(n1),n1=ny1,ny2)
01839     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float32" Name="Z" format="appended" offset="'//&
01840                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
01841     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01842     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = (nz2-nz1+1)*BYR4P)
01843     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'R4',(nz2-nz1+1)
01844     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(Z(n1),n1=nz1,nz2)
01845     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2  ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Coordinates>'//end_rec
01846   case(binary)
01847     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'//trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
01848                                                               trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
01849                                                               trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'">'
01850     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01851     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Coordinates>'
01852     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01853     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float32" Name="X" format="binary">'
01854     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01855     call pack_data(a1=[int((nx2-nx1+1)*BYR4P,I4P)],a2=X,packed=XYZp)
01856     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=XYZp,code=XYZ64)
01857     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(XYZ64)//end_rec
01858     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
01859     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float32" Name="Y" format="binary">'
01860     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01861     call pack_data(a1=[int((ny2-ny1+1)*BYR4P,I4P)],a2=Y,packed=XYZp)
01862     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=XYZp,code=XYZ64)
01863     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(XYZ64)//end_rec
01864     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
01865     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float32" Name="Z" format="binary">'
01866     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01867     call pack_data(a1=[int((nz2-nz1+1)*BYR4P,I4P)],a2=Z,packed=XYZp)
01868     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=XYZp,code=XYZ64) ; deallocate(XYZp)
01869     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(XYZ64)//end_rec ; deallocate(XYZ64)
01870     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
01871     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
01872     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Coordinates>'//end_rec
01873   endselect
01874   return
01875   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01876   endfunction VTK_GEO_XML_RECT_R4
01877 
01880   function VTK_GEO_XML_UNST_R8(NN,NC,X,Y,Z,cf) result(E_IO)
01881   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01882   implicit none
01883   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NN       !< Number of nodes.
01884   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NC       !< Number of cells.
01885   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           X(1:NN)  !< X coordinates.
01886   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           Y(1:NN)  !< Y coordinates.
01887   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           Z(1:NN)  !< Z coordinates.
01888   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf       !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
01889   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO     !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
01890   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer !< Buffer string.
01891   real(R8P), allocatable::             XYZa(:)  !< X, Y, Z coordinates.
01892   integer(I1P), allocatable::          XYZp(:)  !< Packed data.
01893   character(1), allocatable::          XYZ64(:) !< X, Y, Z coordinates encoded in base64.
01894   integer(I4P)::                       rf       !< Real file index.
01895   integer(I4P)::                       n1       !< Counter.
01896   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01897 
01898   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01899   E_IO = -1_I4P
01900   rf = f
01901   if (present(cf)) then
01902     rf = cf ; f = cf
01903   endif
01904   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
01905   case(ascii)
01906     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece NumberOfPoints="'//trim(str(n=NN))//'" NumberOfCells="'//trim(str(n=NC))//'">'
01907     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01908     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01909     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="ascii">'
01910     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
01911     do n1=1,NN
01912       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//str(n=X(n1))//' '//str(n=Y(n1))//' '//str(n=Z(n1))
01913     enddo
01914     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
01915     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'
01916   case(raw,bin_app)
01917     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece NumberOfPoints="'//trim(str(n=NN))//'" NumberOfCells="'//trim(str(n=NC))//'">'
01918     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01919     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01920     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//                                                                  &
01921                '<DataArray type="Float64" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="appended" offset="'// &
01922                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
01923     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01924     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = 3*NN*BYR8P)
01925     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'R8',3*NN
01926     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(X(n1),Y(n1),Z(n1),n1=1,NN)
01927     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'//end_rec
01928   case(binary)
01929     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece NumberOfPoints="'//trim(str(n=NN))//'" NumberOfCells="'//trim(str(n=NC))//'">'
01930     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01931     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Points>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
01932     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points" format="binary">'
01933     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
01934     allocate(XYZa(1:3*NN))
01935     do n1 = 1,NN
01936       XYZa(1+(n1-1)*3:1+(n1-1)*3+2)=[X(n1),Y(n1),Z(n1)]
01937     enddo
01938     call pack_data(a1=[int(3*NN*BYR8P,I4P)],a2=XYZa,packed=XYZp) ; deallocate(XYZa)
01939     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=XYZp,code=XYZ64) ; deallocate(XYZp)
01940     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(XYZ64)//end_rec ; deallocate(XYZ64)
01941     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
01942     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Points>'//end_rec
01943   endselect
01944   return
01945   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
01946   endfunction VTK_GEO_XML_UNST_R8

02155 
02158   function VTK_GEO_XML_CLOSEP(cf) result(E_IO)
02159   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02160   implicit none
02161   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf   !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
02162   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
02163   integer(I4P)::                       rf   !< Real file index.
02164   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02165 
02166   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02167   E_IO = -1_I4P
02168   rf = f
02169   if (present(cf)) then
02170     rf = cf ; f = cf
02171   endif
02172   vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
02173   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
02174   case(ascii)
02175     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Piece>'
02176   case(raw,binary,bin_app)
02177     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Piece>'//end_rec
02178   endselect
02179   return
02180   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02181   endfunction VTK_GEO_XML_CLOSEP
02183 
02226   function VTK_CON_XML(NC,connect,offset,cell_type,idx,cf) result(E_IO)
02227   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02228   implicit none
02229   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NC            !< Number of cells.
02230   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           connect(1:)   !< Mesh connectivity.
02231   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           offset(1:NC)  !< Cell offset.
02232   integer(I1P), intent(IN)::           cell_type(1:) !< VTK cell type.
02233   integer(I1P), intent(IN), optional:: idx           !< Id offset to convert Fortran (first id 1) to C (first id 0) standards.
02234   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf            !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
02235   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO          !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
02236   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer      !< Buffer string.
02237   integer(I1P), allocatable::          cocp(:)       !< Packed data.
02238   character(1), allocatable::          coc64(:)      !< Data encoded in base64.
02239   integer(I1P)::                       incr          !< Actual id offset increment.
02240   integer(I4P)::                       rf            !< Real file index.
02241   integer(I4P)::                       n1            !< Counter.
02242   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02243 
02244   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02245   E_IO = -1_I4P
02246   rf = f
02247   if (present(cf)) then
02248     rf = cf ; f = cf
02249   endif
02250   incr = 0_I1P
02251   if (present(idx)) then
02252     incr = idx
02253   endif
02254   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
02255   case(ascii)
02256     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Cells>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
02257     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//&
02258                                                '<DataArray type="Int32" Name="connectivity" format="ascii">'
02259     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt=FI4P, iostat=E_IO)(connect(n1)+incr,n1=1,offset(NC))
02260     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'
02261     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int32" Name="offsets" format="ascii">'
02262     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt=FI4P, iostat=E_IO)(offset(n1),n1=1,NC)
02263     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'
02264     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int8" Name="types" format="ascii">'
02265     if (lbound(cell_type,dim=1)==ubound(cell_type,dim=1)) then
02266       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt=FI1P, iostat=E_IO)(cell_type(1),n1=1,NC)
02267     else
02268       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt=FI1P, iostat=E_IO)(cell_type(n1),n1=1,NC)
02269     endif
02270     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
02271     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Cells>'
02272   case(raw,bin_app)
02273     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Cells>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
02274     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int32" Name="connectivity" format="appended" offset="'// &
02275                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
02276     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
02277     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = offset(NC)*BYI4P)
02278     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'I4',offset(NC)
02279     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(connect(n1)+incr,n1=1,offset(NC))
02280     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int32" Name="offsets" format="appended" offset="'// &
02281                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
02282     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
02283     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = NC*BYI4P)
02284     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'I4',NC
02285     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(offset(n1),n1=1,NC)
02286     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int8" Name="types" format="appended" offset="'// &
02287                trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
02288     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
02289     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = NC*BYI1P)
02290     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'I1',NC
02291     if (lbound(cell_type,dim=1)==ubound(cell_type,dim=1)) then
02292       write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(cell_type(1),n1=1,NC)
02293     else
02294       write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(cell_type(n1),n1=1,NC)
02295     endif
02296     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Cells>'//end_rec
02297   case(binary)
02298     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Cells>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
02299     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//&
02300                                      '<DataArray type="Int32" Name="connectivity" format="binary">'//end_rec
02301     cocp = transfer([int(offset(NC)*BYI4P,I4P),connect],cocp)
02302     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=cocp,code=coc64)
02303     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(coc64)//end_rec
02304     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
02305     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int32" Name="offsets" format="binary">'//end_rec
02306     cocp = transfer([int(NC*BYI4P,I4P),offset],cocp)
02307     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=cocp,code=coc64)
02308     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(coc64)//end_rec
02309     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
02310     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int8" Name="types" format="binary">'//end_rec
02311     if (lbound(cell_type,dim=1)==ubound(cell_type,dim=1)) then
02312       call pack_data(a1=[int(NC*BYI1P,I4P)],a2=[(cell_type(1),n1=1,NC)],packed=cocp)
02313     else
02314       call pack_data(a1=[int(NC*BYI1P,I4P)],a2=cell_type,packed=cocp)
02315     endif
02316     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=cocp,code=coc64) ; deallocate(cocp)
02317     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(coc64)//end_rec ; deallocate(coc64)
02318     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
02319     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</Cells>'//end_rec
02320   endselect
02321   return
02322   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02323   endfunction VTK_CON_XML
02324 
02340   function VTK_DAT_XML(var_location,var_block_action,cf) result(E_IO)
02341   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02342   implicit none
02343   character(*), intent(IN)::           var_location     !< Location of saving variables: CELL or NODE centered.
02344   character(*), intent(IN)::           var_block_action !< Variables block action: OPEN or CLOSE block.
02345   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf               !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
02346   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO             !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
02347   integer(I4P)::                       rf               !< Real file index.
02348   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02349 
02350   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02351   E_IO = -1_I4P
02352   rf = f
02353   if (present(cf)) then
02354     rf = cf ; f = cf
02355   endif
02356   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
02357   case(ascii)
02358     select case(trim(Upper_Case(var_location)))
02359     case('CELL')
02360       select case(trim(Upper_Case(var_block_action)))
02361       case('OPEN')
02362         write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<CellData>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
02363       case('CLOSE')
02364         vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</CellData>'
02365       endselect
02366     case('NODE')
02367       select case(trim(Upper_Case(var_block_action)))
02368       case('OPEN')
02369         write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<PointData>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
02370       case('CLOSE')
02371         vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</PointData>'
02372       endselect
02373     endselect
02374   case(raw,binary,bin_app)
02375     select case(trim(Upper_Case(var_location)))
02376     case('CELL')
02377       select case(trim(Upper_Case(var_block_action)))
02378       case('OPEN')
02379         write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<CellData>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
02380       case('CLOSE')
02381         vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</CellData>'//end_rec
02382       endselect
02383     case('NODE')
02384       select case(trim(Upper_Case(var_block_action)))
02385       case('OPEN')
02386         write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<PointData>'//end_rec ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
02387       case('CLOSE')
02388         vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</PointData>'//end_rec
02389       endselect
02390     endselect
02391   endselect
02392   return
02393   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02394   endfunction VTK_DAT_XML

02401   function VTK_VAR_XML_SCAL_R8(NC_NN,varname,var,cf) result(E_IO)
02402   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02403   implicit none
02404   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NC_NN        !< Number of cells or nodes.
02405   character(*), intent(IN)::           varname      !< Variable name.
02406   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           var(1:NC_NN) !< Variable to be saved.
02407   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf           !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
02408   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO         !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
02409   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer     !< Buffer string.
02410   integer(I1P), allocatable::          varp(:)      !< Packed data.
02411   character(1), allocatable::          var64(:)     !< Variable encoded in base64.
02412   integer(I4P)::                       rf           !< Real file index.
02413   integer(I4P)::                       n1           !< Counter.
02414   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02415 
02416   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02417   E_IO = -1_I4P
02418   rf = f
02419   if (present(cf)) then
02420     rf = cf ; f = cf
02421   endif
02422   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
02423   case(ascii)
02424     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" Name="'//trim(varname)//&
02425                '" NumberOfComponents="1" format="ascii">'
02426     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
02427     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A,'//trim(str(.true.,NC_NN))//'(1X,'//FR8P//'))',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent),&
02428                                                                                             (var(n1),n1=1,NC_NN)
02429     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'
02430   case(raw,bin_app)
02431     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" Name="'//trim(varname)//&
02432                '" NumberOfComponents="1" format="appended" offset="'//trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
02433     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
02434     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = NC_NN*BYR8P)
02435     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'R8',NC_NN
02436     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)var
02437   case(binary)
02438     s_buffer=repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" Name="'//trim(varname)//&
02439              '" NumberOfComponents="1" format="binary">'
02440     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
02441     call pack_data(a1=[int(NC_NN*BYR8P,I4P)],a2=var,packed=varp)
02442     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=varp,code=var64) ; deallocate(varp)
02443     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(var64)//end_rec ; deallocate(var64)
02444     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
02445   endselect
02446   return
02447   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02448   endfunction VTK_VAR_XML_SCAL_R8
02449 
02452   function VTK_VAR_XML_SCAL_R4(NC_NN,varname,var,cf) result(E_IO)
02453   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

02488   case(binary)

02490              '" NumberOfComponents="1" format="binary">'
02491     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
02492     call pack_data(a1=[int(NC_NN*BYR4P,I4P)],a2=var,packed=varp)
02493     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=varp,code=var64) ; deallocate(varp)
02494     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(var64)//end_rec ; deallocate(var64)
02495     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
02496   endselect
02497   return
02498   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02499   endfunction VTK_VAR_XML_SCAL_R4

02503   function VTK_VAR_XML_SCAL_I8(NC_NN,varname,var,cf) result(E_IO)
02504   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02505   implicit none
02506   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NC_NN        !< Number of cells or nodes.
02507   character(*), intent(IN)::           varname      !< Variable name.
02508   integer(I8P), intent(IN)::           var(1:NC_NN) !< Variable to be saved.
02509   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf           !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
02510   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO         !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
02511   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer     !< Buffer string.
02512   integer(I1P), allocatable::          varp(:)      !< Packed data.
02513   character(1), allocatable::          var64(:)     !< Variable encoded in base64.
02514   integer(I4P)::                       rf           !< Real file index.
02515   integer(I4P)::                       n1           !< Counter.
02516   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02517 
02518   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02519   E_IO = -1_I4P
02520   rf = f

02522     rf = cf ; f = cf
02523   endif

02527                '" NumberOfComponents="1" format="ascii">'
02528     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
02529     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A,'//trim(str(.true.,NC_NN))//'(1X,'//FI8P//'))',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent),&
02530                                                                                             (var(n1),n1=1,NC_NN)
02531     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)'</DataArray>'
02532   case(raw,bin_app)
02533     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int64" Name="'//trim(varname)//&
02534                '" NumberOfComponents="1" format="appended" offset="'//trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
02535     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
02536     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = int(NC_NN*BYI8P,I4P))
02537     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'I8',NC_NN
02538     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)var
02539   case(binary)
02540     s_buffer=repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int64" Name="'//trim(varname)//&
02541              '" NumberOfComponents="1" format="binary">'
02542     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
02543     call pack_data(a1=[int(NC_NN*BYI8P,I4P)],a2=var,packed=varp)
02544     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=varp,code=var64) ; deallocate(varp)
02545     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(var64)//end_rec ; deallocate(var64)
02546     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
02547   endselect
02548   return
02549   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02550   endfunction VTK_VAR_XML_SCAL_I8

02554   function VTK_VAR_XML_SCAL_I4(NC_NN,varname,var,cf) result(E_IO)
02555   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02556   implicit none
02557   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NC_NN        !< Number of cells or nodes.
02558   character(*), intent(IN)::           varname      !< Variable name.
02559   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           var(1:NC_NN) !< Variable to be saved.
02560   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf           !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
02561   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO         !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
02562   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer     !< Buffer string.
02563   integer(I1P), allocatable::          varp(:)      !< Packed data.
02564   character(1), allocatable::          var64(:)     !< Variable encoded in base64.
02565   integer(I4P)::                       rf           !< Real file index.
02566   integer(I4P)::                       n1           !< Counter.
02567   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02568 
02569   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02570   E_IO = -1_I4P
02571   rf = f
02572   if (present(cf)) then
02573     rf = cf ; f = cf
02574   endif
02575   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
02576   case(ascii)
02577     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int32" Name="'//trim(varname)//&
02578                '" NumberOfComponents="1" format="ascii">'
02579     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
02580     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A,'//trim(str(.true.,NC_NN))//'(1X,'//FI4P//'))',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent),&
02581                                                                                             (var(n1),n1=1,NC_NN)
02582     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'
02583   case(raw,bin_app)
02584     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int32" Name="'//trim(varname)// &
02585                '" NumberOfComponents="1" format="appended" offset="'//trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
02586     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
02587     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = NC_NN*BYI4P)
02588     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'I4',NC_NN
02589     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)var
02590   case(binary)
02591     s_buffer=repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int32" Name="'//trim(varname)// &
02592              '" NumberOfComponents="1" format="binary">'
02593     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
02594     varp = transfer([int(NC_NN*BYI4P,I4P),var],varp)
02595     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=varp,code=var64) ; deallocate(varp)
02596     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(var64)//end_rec ; deallocate(var64)
02597     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
02598   endselect
02599   return
02600   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02601   endfunction VTK_VAR_XML_SCAL_I4

02706   function VTK_VAR_XML_VECT_R8(NC_NN,varname,varX,varY,varZ,cf) result(E_IO)
02707   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02708   implicit none
02709   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NC_NN         !< Number of cells or nodes.
02710   character(*), intent(IN)::           varname       !< Variable name.
02711   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           varX(1:NC_NN) !< X component.
02712   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           varY(1:NC_NN) !< Y component.
02713   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           varZ(1:NC_NN) !< Z component.
02714   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf            !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
02715   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO          !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
02716   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer      !< Buffer string.
02717   real(R8P),    allocatable::          var(:)        !< X, Y, Z component.
02718   integer(I1P), allocatable::          varp(:)       !< Packed data.
02719   character(1), allocatable::          var64(:)      !< Variable encoded in base64.
02720   integer(I4P)::                       rf            !< Real file index.
02721   integer(I4P)::                       n1            !< Counter.

02723 
02724   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

02728     rf = cf ; f = cf
02729   endif
02730   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
02731   case(ascii)
02732     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" Name="'//trim(varname)//&
02733                '" NumberOfComponents="3" format="ascii">'
02734     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
02735     do n1=1,NC_NN
02736       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A,3(1X,'//FR8P//'))',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent),&
02737                                                                   varX(n1),varY(n1),varZ(n1)
02738     enddo
02739     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'
02740   case(raw,bin_app)

02742                '" NumberOfComponents="3" format="appended" offset="'//trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
02743     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
02744     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = 3*NC_NN*BYR8P)

02747   case(binary)

02749                '" NumberOfComponents="3" format="binary">'
02750     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
02751     allocate(var(1:3*NC_NN))

02753       var(1+(n1-1)*3:1+(n1-1)*3+2)=[varX(n1),varY(n1),varZ(n1)]
02754     enddo

02897   integer(I4P), allocatable::          var(:)        !< X, Y, Z component.
02898   integer(I1P), allocatable::          varp(:)       !< Packed data.
02899   character(1), allocatable::          var64(:)      !< Variable encoded in base64.
02900   integer(I4P)::                       rf            !< Real file index.
02901   integer(I4P)::                       n1            !< Counter.
02902   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02903 
02904   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
02905   E_IO = -1_I4P
02906   rf = f
02907   if (present(cf)) then
02908     rf = cf ; f = cf
02909   endif
02910   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
02911   case(ascii)
02912     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int32" Name="'//trim(varname)//&
02913                '" NumberOfComponents="3" format="ascii">'
02914     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
02915     do n1=1,NC_NN
02916       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A,3(1X,'//FI4P//'))',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent),&
02917                                                                   varX(n1),varY(n1),varZ(n1)
02918     enddo
02919     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'
02920   case(raw,bin_app)
02921     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int32" Name="'//trim(varname)//&
02922                '" NumberOfComponents="3" format="appended" offset="'//trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
02923     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
02924     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = 3*NC_NN*BYI4P)
02925     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'I4',3*NC_NN
02926     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(varX(n1),varY(n1),varZ(n1),n1=1,NC_NN)
02927   case(binary)
02928     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int32" Name="'//trim(varname)//&
02929                '" NumberOfComponents="3" format="binary">'
02930     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
02931     allocate(var(1:3*NC_NN))
02932     do n1=1,NC_NN
02933       var(1+(n1-1)*3:1+(n1-1)*3+2)=[varX(n1),varY(n1),varZ(n1)]
02934     enddo
02935     varp = transfer([int(3*NC_NN*BYI4P,I4P),var],varp) ; deallocate(var)
02936     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=varp,code=var64) ; deallocate(varp)

02938     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
02939   endselect

03066   function VTK_VAR_XML_LIST_R8(NC_NN,N_COL,varname,var,cf) result(E_IO)
03067   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03068   implicit none
03069   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NC_NN      !< Number of cells or nodes.
03070   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           N_COL      !< Number of columns.
03071   character(*), intent(IN)::           varname    !< Variable name.
03072   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           var(1:,1:) !< Components [1:N_COL,1:NC_NN].
03073   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf         !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
03074   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO       !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
03075   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer   !< Buffer string.
03076   real(R8P),    allocatable::          var1(:)    !< One-dimensionalized data.
03077   integer(I1P), allocatable::          varp(:)    !< Packed data.
03078   character(1), allocatable::          var64(:)   !< Variable encoded in base64.
03079   integer(I4P)::                       rf         !< Real file index.
03080   integer(I4P)::                       n1,n2      !< Counters.
03081   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03082 
03083   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03084   E_IO = -1_I4P
03085   rf = f
03086   if (present(cf)) then
03087     rf = cf ; f = cf
03088   endif
03089   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
03090   case(ascii)
03091     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" Name="'//trim(varname)//'" NumberOfComponents="'// &
03092                trim(str(.true.,N_COL))//'" format="ascii">'
03093     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
03094     do n2=1,NC_NN
03095       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A,'//trim(str(.true.,N_COL))//'(1X,'//FR8P//'))',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent),&
03096                                                                                               (var(n1,n2),n1=1,N_COL)
03097     enddo
03098     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'
03099   case(raw,bin_app)
03100     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" Name="'//trim(varname)//'" NumberOfComponents="'// &
03101                trim(str(.true.,N_COL))//'" format="appended" offset="'//trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
03102     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
03103     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = N_COL*NC_NN*BYR8P)
03104     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'R8',N_COL*NC_NN
03105     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)var
03106   case(binary)
03107     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Float64" Name="'//trim(varname)//'" NumberOfComponents="'// &
03108                trim(str(.true.,N_COL))//'" format="binary">'
03109     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
03110     allocate(var1(1:NC_NN*N_COL))
03111     do n2=1,NC_NN
03112       var1(1+(n2-1)*N_COL:1+(n2-1)*N_COL+N_COL-1)=var(:,n2)
03113     enddo
03114     call pack_data(a1=[int(N_COL*NC_NN*BYR8P,I4P)],a2=var1,packed=varp) ; deallocate(var1)
03115     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=varp,code=var64) ; deallocate(varp)
03116     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(var64)//end_rec ; deallocate(var64)
03117     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
03118   endselect
03119   return
03120   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03121   endfunction VTK_VAR_XML_LIST_R8

03232     call pack_data(a1=[int(N_COL*NC_NN*BYI8P,I4P)],a2=var1,packed=varp) ; deallocate(var1)
03233     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=varp,code=var64) ; deallocate(varp)
03234     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(var64)//end_rec ; deallocate(var64)
03235     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
03236   endselect
03237   return
03238   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03239   endfunction VTK_VAR_XML_LIST_I8
03240 
03243   function VTK_VAR_XML_LIST_I4(NC_NN,N_COL,varname,var,cf) result(E_IO)
03244   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03245   implicit none
03246   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NC_NN      !< Number of cells or nodes.
03247   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           N_COL      !< Number of columns.
03248   character(*), intent(IN)::           varname    !< Variable name.
03249   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           var(1:,1:) !< Components [1:N_COL,1:NC_NN].
03250   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf         !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
03251   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO       !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
03252   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer   !< Buffer string.
03253   integer(I4P), allocatable::          var1(:)    !< One-dimensionalized data.
03254   integer(I1P), allocatable::          varp(:)    !< Packed data.
03255   character(1), allocatable::          var64(:)   !< Variable encoded in base64.
03256   integer(I4P)::                       rf         !< Real file index.
03257   integer(I4P)::                       n1,n2      !< Counters.
03258   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03259 
03260   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03261   E_IO = -1_I4P
03262   rf = f
03263   if (present(cf)) then
03264     rf = cf ; f = cf
03265   endif
03266   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
03267   case(ascii)
03268     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int32" Name="'//trim(varname)//'" NumberOfComponents="'// &
03269                trim(str(.true.,N_COL))//'" format="ascii">'
03270     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
03271     do n2=1,NC_NN
03272       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A,'//trim(str(.true.,N_COL))//'(1X,'//FI4P//'))',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent),&
03273                                                                                               (var(n1,n2),n1=1,N_COL)
03274     enddo
03275     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'
03276   case(raw,bin_app)
03277     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int32" Name="'//trim(varname)//'" NumberOfComponents="'// &
03278                trim(str(.true.,N_COL))//'" format="appended" offset="'//trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
03279     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
03280     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = N_COL*NC_NN*BYI4P)
03281     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'I4',N_COL*NC_NN
03282     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)var
03283   case(binary)
03284     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int32" Name="'//trim(varname)//'" NumberOfComponents="'// &
03285                trim(str(.true.,N_COL))//'" format="binary">'
03286     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
03287     allocate(var1(1:NC_NN*N_COL))
03288     do n2=1,NC_NN
03289       var1(1+(n2-1)*N_COL:1+(n2-1)*N_COL+N_COL-1)=var(:,n2)
03290     enddo
03291     varp = transfer([int(N_COL*NC_NN*BYI4P,I4P),var1],varp)
03292     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=varp,code=var64) ; deallocate(varp)
03293     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(var64)//end_rec ; deallocate(var64)
03294     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
03295   endselect
03296   return
03297   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03298   endfunction VTK_VAR_XML_LIST_I4
03299

03303   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

03305   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NC_NN      !< Number of cells or nodes.
03306   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           N_COL      !< Number of columns.

03309   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf         !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
03310   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO       !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
03311   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer   !< Buffer string.
03312   integer(I2P), allocatable::          var1(:)    !< One-dimensionalized data.
03313   integer(I1P), allocatable::          varp(:)    !< Packed data.

03316   integer(I4P)::                       n1,n2      !< Counters.
03317   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

03324   endif
03325   select case(vtk(rf)%f)

03337                trim(str(.true.,N_COL))//'" format="appended" offset="'//trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'

03340     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'I2',N_COL*NC_NN

03346     allocate(var1(1:NC_NN*N_COL))
03347     do n2=1,NC_NN

03349     enddo
03350     call pack_data(a1=[int(N_COL*NC_NN*BYI2P,I4P)],a2=var1,packed=varp) ; deallocate(var1)

03367   integer(I1P), intent(IN)::           var(1:,1:) !< Components [1:N_COL,1:NC_NN].
03368   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf         !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
03369   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO       !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
03370   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer   !< Buffer string.
03371   integer(I1P), allocatable::          var1(:)    !< One-dimensionalized data.
03372   integer(I1P), allocatable::          varp(:)    !< Packed data.

03394   case(raw,bin_app)
03395     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int8" Name="'//trim(varname)//'" NumberOfComponents="'// &
03396                trim(str(.true.,N_COL))//'" format="appended" offset="'//trim(str(.true.,vtk(rf)%ioffset))//'"/>'
03397     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
03398     call vtk(rf)%byte_update(N_Byte = N_COL*NC_NN*BYI1P)
03399     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,'I1',N_COL*NC_NN
03400     write(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)var
03401   case(binary)
03402     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<DataArray type="Int8" Name="'//trim(varname)//'" NumberOfComponents="'// &
03403                trim(str(.true.,N_COL))//'" format="binary">'
