03405     allocate(var1(1:NC_NN*N_COL))
03406     do n2=1,NC_NN
03407       var1(1+(n2-1)*N_COL:1+(n2-1)*N_COL+N_COL-1)=var(:,n2)
03408     enddo
03409     call pack_data(a1=[int(N_COL*NC_NN*BYI1P,I4P)],a2=var1,packed=varp) ; deallocate(var1)
03410     call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=varp,code=var64) ; deallocate(varp)
03411     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent+2)//tochar(var64)//end_rec ; deallocate(var64)
03412     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</DataArray>'//end_rec
03413   endselect
03414   return
03415   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03416   endfunction VTK_VAR_XML_LIST_I1
03418 
03426   function VTK_END_XML(cf) result(E_IO)
03427   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03428   implicit none
03429   integer(I4P), intent(INOUT), optional:: cf       !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
03430   integer(I4P)::                          E_IO     !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
03431   character(2)::                          var_type !< Varable type = R8,R4,I8,I4,I2,I1.
03432   real(R8P),    allocatable::             v_R8(:)  !< R8 vector for IO in AppendData.
03433   real(R4P),    allocatable::             v_R4(:)  !< R4 vector for IO in AppendData.
03434   integer(I8P), allocatable::             v_I8(:)  !< I8 vector for IO in AppendData.
03435   integer(I4P), allocatable::             v_I4(:)  !< I4 vector for IO in AppendData.
03436   integer(I2P), allocatable::             v_I2(:)  !< I2 vector for IO in AppendData.
03437   integer(I1P), allocatable::             v_I1(:)  !< I1 vector for IO in AppendData.
03438   integer(I1P), allocatable::             varp(:)  !< Packed data.
03439   character(1), allocatable::             var64(:) !< Variable encoded in base64.
03440   integer(I4P)::                          rf       !< Real file index.
03441 #ifdef HUGE
03442   integer(I8P)::                          N_v      !< Vector dimension.
03443   integer(I8P)::                          n1       !< Counter.
03444 #else
03445   integer(I4P)::                          N_v      !< Vector dimension.
03446   integer(I4P)::                          n1       !< Counter.
03447 #endif
03448   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03449 
03450   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03451   E_IO = -1_I4P
03452   rf = f
03453   if (present(cf)) then
03454     rf = cf ; f = cf
03455   endif
03456   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
03457   case(ascii)
03458     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
03459     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//'>'
03460     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)'</VTKFile>'
03461   case(raw,bin_app)
03462     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
03463     write(unit  =vtk(rf)%u, iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//'>'//end_rec
03464     if (vtk(rf)%f==raw) then
03465       write(unit  =vtk(rf)%u, iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<AppendedData encoding="raw">'//end_rec
03466     else
03467       write(unit  =vtk(rf)%u, iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<AppendedData encoding="base64">'//end_rec
03468     endif
03469     write(unit  =vtk(rf)%u, iostat=E_IO)'_'
03470     endfile(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)
03471     rewind(unit =vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)
03472     do
03473       read(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO,end=100)vtk(rf)%N_Byte,var_type,N_v
03474       select case(var_type)
03475       case('R8')
03476         allocate(v_R8(1:N_v))
03477         read(unit =vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(v_R8(n1),n1=1,N_v)
03478         if (vtk(rf)%f==raw) then
03479           write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)int(vtk(rf)%N_Byte,I4P),(v_R8(n1),n1=1,N_v)
03480         else
03481           call pack_data(a1=[int(vtk(rf)%N_Byte,I4P)],a2=v_R8,packed=varp)
03482           call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=varp,code=var64) ; deallocate(varp)
03483           write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)tochar(var64) ; deallocate(var64)
03484         endif
03485         deallocate(v_R8)
03486       case('R4')
03487         allocate(v_R4(1:N_v))
03488         read(unit =vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(v_R4(n1),n1=1,N_v)
03489         if (vtk(rf)%f==raw) then
03490           write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)int(vtk(rf)%N_Byte,I4P),(v_R4(n1),n1=1,N_v)
03491         else
03492           call pack_data(a1=[int(vtk(rf)%N_Byte,I4P)],a2=v_R4,packed=varp)
03493           call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=varp,code=var64) ; deallocate(varp)
03494           write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)tochar(var64) ; deallocate(var64)
03495         endif
03496         deallocate(v_R4)
03497       case('I8')
03498         allocate(v_I8(1:N_v))
03499         read(unit =vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(v_I8(n1),n1=1,N_v)
03500         if (vtk(rf)%f==raw) then
03501           write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)int(vtk(rf)%N_Byte,I4P),(v_I8(n1),n1=1,N_v)
03502         else
03503           call pack_data(a1=[int(vtk(rf)%N_Byte,I4P)],a2=v_I8,packed=varp)
03504           call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=varp,code=var64) ; deallocate(varp)
03505           write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)tochar(var64) ; deallocate(var64)
03506         endif
03507         deallocate(v_I8)
03508       case('I4')
03509         allocate(v_I4(1:N_v))
03510         read(unit =vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(v_I4(n1),n1=1,N_v)
03511         if (vtk(rf)%f==raw) then
03512           write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)int(vtk(rf)%N_Byte,I4P),(v_I4(n1),n1=1,N_v)
03513         else
03514           varp = transfer([int(vtk(rf)%N_Byte,I4P),v_I4],varp)
03515           call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=varp,code=var64) ; deallocate(varp)
03516           write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)tochar(var64) ; deallocate(var64)
03517         endif
03518         deallocate(v_I4)
03519       case('I2')
03520         allocate(v_I2(1:N_v))
03521         read(unit =vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(v_I2(n1),n1=1,N_v)
03522         if (vtk(rf)%f==raw) then
03523           write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)int(vtk(rf)%N_Byte,I4P),(v_I2(n1),n1=1,N_v)
03524         else
03525           call pack_data(a1=[int(vtk(rf)%N_Byte,I4P)],a2=v_I2,packed=varp)
03526           call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=varp,code=var64) ; deallocate(varp)
03527           write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)tochar(var64) ; deallocate(var64)
03528         endif
03529         deallocate(v_I2)
03530       case('I1')
03531         allocate(v_I1(1:N_v))
03532         read(unit =vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)(v_I1(n1),n1=1,N_v)
03533         if (vtk(rf)%f==raw) then
03534           write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)int(vtk(rf)%N_Byte,I4P),(v_I1(n1),n1=1,N_v)
03535         else
03536           call pack_data(a1=[int(vtk(rf)%N_Byte,I4P)],a2=v_I1,packed=varp)
03537           call b64_encode(nB=int(BYI1P,I4P),n=varp,code=var64) ; deallocate(varp)
03538           write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)tochar(var64) ; deallocate(var64)
03539         endif
03540         deallocate(v_I1)
03541       case default
03542         E_IO = 1
03543         write (stderr,'(A)')' bad var_type = '//var_type
03544         write (stderr,'(A)')' N_Byte = '//trim(str(n=vtk(rf)%N_Byte))//' N_v = '//trim(str(n=N_v))
03545         return
03546       endselect
03547     enddo
03548     100 continue
03549     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)end_rec
03550     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</AppendedData>'//end_rec
03551     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'</VTKFile>'//end_rec
03552     close(unit=vtk(rf)%ua,iostat=E_IO)
03553   case(binary)
03554     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
03555     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//'>'//end_rec
03556     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'</VTKFile>'//end_rec
03557   endselect
03558   close(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)
03559   call vtk_update(act='remove',cf=rf,Nvtk=Nvtk,vtk=vtk)
03560   f = rf
03561   if (present(cf)) cf = rf
03562   return
03563   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03564   endfunction VTK_END_XML
03565 
03569   function VTM_INI_XML(filename) result(E_IO)
03570   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03571   implicit none
03572   character(*), intent(IN):: filename !< File name of output VTM file.
03573   integer(I4P)::             E_IO     !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
03574   character(len=maxlen)::    s_buffer !< Buffer string.
03575   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03576 
03577   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03578   E_IO = -1_I4P
03579   if (.not.ir_initialized) call IR_Init
03580   if (endian==endianL) then
03581     s_buffer='<VTKFile type="vtkMultiBlockDataSet" version="1.0" byte_order="LittleEndian">'
03582   else
03583     s_buffer='<VTKFile type="vtkMultiBlockDataSet" version="1.0" byte_order="BigEndian">'
03584   endif
03585   open(unit=Get_Unit(vtm%u),file=trim(filename),form='FORMATTED',access='SEQUENTIAL',action='WRITE',status='REPLACE',iostat=E_IO)
03586   write(unit=vtm%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)'<?xml version="1.0"?>'
03587   write(unit=vtm%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtm%indent = 2
03588   write(unit=vtm%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtm%indent)//'<vtkMultiBlockDataSet>' ; vtm%indent = vtm%indent + 2
03589   vtm%blk = -1
03590   return
03591   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03592   endfunction VTM_INI_XML
03593 
03597   function VTM_BLK_XML(block_action) result(E_IO)
03598   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03599   implicit none
03600   character(*), intent(IN):: block_action !< Block action: OPEN or CLOSE block.
03601   integer(I4P)::             E_IO         !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
03602   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03603 
03604   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03605   E_IO = -1_I4P
03606   select case(trim(Upper_Case(block_action)))
03607   case('OPEN')
03608     vtm%blk = vtm%blk + 1
03609     write(unit=vtm%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtm%indent)//'<Block index="'//trim(str(.true.,vtm%blk))//'">'
03610     vtm%indent = vtm%indent + 2
03611   case('CLOSE')
03612     vtm%indent = vtm%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtm%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtm%indent)//'</Block>'
03613   endselect
03614   return
03615   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03616   endfunction VTM_BLK_XML
03617 
03621   function VTM_WRF_XML(flist) result(E_IO)
03622   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03623   implicit none
03624   character(*), intent(IN):: flist(:) !< List of VTK-XML wrapped files.
03625   integer(I4P)::             E_IO     !< Input/Output inquiring flag: 0 if IO is done, > 0 if IO is not done.
03626   integer(I4P)::             f        !< File counter.
03627   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03628 
03629   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03630   E_IO = -1_I4P
03631   do f=1,size(flist)
03632     write(unit=vtm%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtm%indent)//'<DataSet index="'//trim(str(.true.,f-1))//'" file="'// &
03633                                            adjustl(trim(flist(f)))//'"/>'
03634   enddo
03635   return
03636   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03637   endfunction VTM_WRF_XML
03638 
03643   function VTM_END_XML() result(E_IO)
03644   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03645   implicit none
03646   integer(I4P):: E_IO !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
03647   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03648 
03649   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03650   E_IO = -1_I4P
03651   vtm%indent = vtm%indent - 2
03652   write(unit=vtm%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtm%indent)//'</vtkMultiBlockDataSet>'
03653   write(unit=vtm%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)'</VTKFile>'
03654   close(unit=vtm%u)
03655   return
03656   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03657   endfunction VTM_END_XML

03662   function PVTK_INI_XML(filename,mesh_topology,tp,cf,nx1,nx2,ny1,ny2,nz1,nz2) result(E_IO)
03663   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03664   implicit none
03665   character(*), intent(IN)::            filename      !< File name.
03666   character(*), intent(IN)::            mesh_topology !< Mesh topology.
03667   character(*), intent(IN)::            tp            !< Type of geometry representation (Float32, Float64, ecc).
03668   integer(I4P), intent(OUT), optional:: cf            !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
03669   integer(I4P), intent(IN),  optional:: nx1           !< Initial node of x axis.
03670   integer(I4P), intent(IN),  optional:: nx2           !< Final node of x axis.
03671   integer(I4P), intent(IN),  optional:: ny1           !< Initial node of y axis.
03672   integer(I4P), intent(IN),  optional:: ny2           !< Final node of y axis.
03673   integer(I4P), intent(IN),  optional:: nz1           !< Initial node of z axis.
03674   integer(I4P), intent(IN),  optional:: nz2           !< Final node of z axis.
03675   integer(I4P)::                        E_IO          !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
03676   character(len=maxlen)::               s_buffer      !< Buffer string.
03677   integer(I4P)::                        rf            !< Real file index.
03678   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03679 
03680   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03681   E_IO = -1_I4P
03682   if (.not.ir_initialized) call IR_Init
03683   call vtk_update(act='add',cf=rf,Nvtk=Nvtk,vtk=vtk)
03684   f = rf
03685   if (present(cf)) cf = rf
03686   vtk(rf)%topology = trim(mesh_topology)
03687   open(unit=Get_Unit(vtk(rf)%u),file=trim(filename),&
03688        form='FORMATTED',access='SEQUENTIAL',action='WRITE',status='REPLACE',iostat=E_IO)
03689   write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)'<?xml version="1.0"?>'
03690   if (endian==endianL) then
03691     s_buffer = '<VTKFile type="'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//'" version="0.1" byte_order="LittleEndian">'
03692   else
03693     s_buffer = '<VTKFile type="'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//'" version="0.1" byte_order="BigEndian">'
03694   endif
03695   write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtk(rf)%indent = 2
03696   select case(trim(vtk(rf)%topology))
03697   case('PRectilinearGrid')
03698     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//' WholeExtent="'//&
03699                trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '//                             &
03700                trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '//                             &
03701                trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'" GhostLevel="#">'
03702     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
03703     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<PCoordinates>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
03704     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<PDataArray type="'//trim(tp)//'"/>'
03705     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<PDataArray type="'//trim(tp)//'"/>'
03706     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<PDataArray type="'//trim(tp)//'"/>'
03707     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</PCoordinates>'
03708   case('PStructuredGrid')
03709     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//' WholeExtent="'//&
03710                trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '//                             &
03711                trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '//                             &
03712                trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'" GhostLevel="#">'
03713     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
03714     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<PPoints>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
03715     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<PDataArray type="'//trim(tp)//'" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points"/>'
03716     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
03717     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</PPoints>'
03718   case('PUnstructuredGrid')
03719     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//' GhostLevel="0">'
03720     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer) ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
03721     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<PPoints>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
03722     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<PDataArray type="'//trim(tp)//'" NumberOfComponents="3" Name="Points"/>'
03723     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
03724     vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</PPoints>'
03725   endselect
03726   return
03727   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03728   endfunction PVTK_INI_XML
03729 
03733   function PVTK_GEO_XML(source,cf,nx1,nx2,ny1,ny2,nz1,nz2) result(E_IO)
03734   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03735   implicit none
03736   character(*), intent(IN)::           source   !< Source file name containing the piece data.
03737   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf       !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
03738   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: nx1      !< Initial node of x axis.
03739   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: nx2      !< Final node of x axis.
03740   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: ny1      !< Initial node of y axis.
03741   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: ny2      !< Final node of y axis.
03742   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: nz1      !< Initial node of z axis.
03743   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: nz2      !< Final node of z axis.
03744   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO     !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
03745   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer !< Buffer string.
03746   integer(I4P)::                       rf       !< Real file index.
03747   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03748 
03749   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03750   E_IO = -1_I4P
03751   rf = f
03752   if (present(cf)) then
03753     rf = cf ; f = cf
03754   endif
03755   select case (vtk(rf)%topology)
03756   case('PRectilinearGrid','PStructuredGrid')
03757     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Extent="'// &
03758                trim(str(n=nx1))//' '//trim(str(n=nx2))//' '// &
03759                trim(str(n=ny1))//' '//trim(str(n=ny2))//' '// &
03760                trim(str(n=nz1))//' '//trim(str(n=nz2))//'" Source="'//trim(source)//'"/>'
03761     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
03762   case('PUnstructuredGrid')
03763     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<Piece Source="'//trim(source)//'"/>'
03764   endselect
03765   return
03766   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03767   endfunction PVTK_GEO_XML

03772   function PVTK_DAT_XML(var_location,var_block_action,cf) result(E_IO)
03773   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03774   implicit none
03775   character(*), intent(IN)::           var_location     !< Location of saving variables: CELL or NODE centered.
03776   character(*), intent(IN)::           var_block_action !< Variables block action: OPEN or CLOSE block.
03777   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf               !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
03778   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO             !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
03779   integer(I4P)::                       rf               !< Real file index.
03780   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03781 
03782   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03783   E_IO = -1_I4P
03784   rf = f
03785   if (present(cf)) then
03786     rf = cf ; f = cf
03787   endif
03788   select case(trim(Upper_Case(var_location)))
03789   case('CELL')
03790     select case(trim(Upper_Case(var_block_action)))
03791     case('OPEN')
03792       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<PCellData>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
03793     case('CLOSE')
03794       vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</PCellData>'
03795     endselect
03796   case('NODE')
03797     select case(trim(Upper_Case(var_block_action)))
03798     case('OPEN')
03799       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<PPointData>' ; vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent + 2
03800     case('CLOSE')
03801       vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2 ; write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</PPointData>'
03802     endselect
03803   endselect
03804   return
03805   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03806   endfunction PVTK_DAT_XML

03811   function PVTK_VAR_XML(varname,tp,cf,Nc) result(E_IO)
03812   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03813   implicit none
03814   character(*), intent(IN)::           varname  !< Variable name.
03815   character(*), intent(IN)::           tp       !< Type of data representation (Float32, Float64, ecc).
03816   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf       !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
03817   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: Nc       !< Number of components of variable.
03818   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO     !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
03819   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer !< Buffer string.
03820   integer(I4P)::                       rf       !< Real file index.
03821   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03822 
03823   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03824   E_IO = -1_I4P
03825   rf = f
03826   if (present(cf)) then
03827     rf = cf ; f = cf
03828   endif
03829   if (present(Nc)) then
03830     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<PDataArray type="'//trim(tp)//'" Name="'//trim(varname)//&
03831                '" NumberOfComponents="'//trim(str(.true.,Nc))//'"/>'
03832   else
03833     s_buffer = repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'<PDataArray type="'//trim(tp)//'" Name="'//trim(varname)//'"/>'
03834   endif
03835   write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)
03836   return
03837   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03838   endfunction PVTK_VAR_XML

03843   function PVTK_END_XML(cf) result(E_IO)
03844   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03845   implicit none
03846   integer(I4P), intent(INOUT), optional:: cf   !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
03847   integer(I4P)::                          E_IO !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
03848   integer(I4P)::                          rf   !< Real file index.
03849   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03850 
03851   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03852   E_IO = -1_I4P
03853   rf = f
03854   if (present(cf)) then
03855     rf = cf ; f = cf
03856   endif
03857   vtk(rf)%indent = vtk(rf)%indent - 2
03858   write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)repeat(' ',vtk(rf)%indent)//'</'//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//'>'
03859   write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)'</VTKFile>'
03860   close(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)
03861   call vtk_update(act='remove',cf=rf,Nvtk=Nvtk,vtk=vtk)
03862   f = rf
03863   if (present(cf)) cf = rf
03864   return
03865   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03866   endfunction PVTK_END_XML

03876   function VTK_INI(output_format,filename,title,mesh_topology,cf) result(E_IO)
03877   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03878   implicit none
03879   character(*), intent(IN)::            output_format !< Output format: ASCII or RAW.
03880   character(*), intent(IN)::            filename      !< Name of file.
03881   character(*), intent(IN)::            title         !< Title.
03882   character(*), intent(IN)::            mesh_topology !< Mesh topology.
03883   integer(I4P), intent(OUT), optional:: cf            !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
03884   integer(I4P)::                        E_IO          !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
03885   integer(I4P)::                        rf            !< Real file index.
03886   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03887 
03888   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03889   E_IO = -1_I4P
03890   if (.not.ir_initialized) call IR_Init
03891   call vtk_update(act='add',cf=rf,Nvtk=Nvtk,vtk=vtk)
03892   f = rf
03893   if (present(cf)) cf = rf
03894   vtk(rf)%topology = trim(mesh_topology)
03895   select case(trim(Upper_Case(output_format)))
03896   case('ASCII')
03897     vtk(rf)%f = ascii
03898     open(unit=Get_Unit(vtk(rf)%u),file=trim(filename),form='FORMATTED',&
03899          access='SEQUENTIAL',action='WRITE',status='REPLACE',iostat=E_IO)
03900     ! writing header of file
03901     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)'# vtk DataFile Version 3.0'
03902     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(title)
03903     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)trim(Upper_Case(output_format))
03904     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)'DATASET '//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)
03905   case('RAW')
03906     vtk(rf)%f = raw
03907     open(unit=Get_Unit(vtk(rf)%u),file=trim(filename),&
03908          form='UNFORMATTED',access='STREAM',action='WRITE',status='REPLACE',iostat=E_IO)
03909     ! writing header of file
03910     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'# vtk DataFile Version 3.0'//end_rec
03911     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(title)//end_rec
03912     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(Upper_Case(output_format))//end_rec
03913     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'DATASET '//trim(vtk(rf)%topology)//end_rec
03914   endselect
03915   return
03916   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03917   endfunction VTK_INI
03918 
03923   function VTK_GEO_STRP_R8(Nx,Ny,Nz,X0,Y0,Z0,Dx,Dy,Dz,cf) result(E_IO)
03924   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03925   implicit none
03926   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           Nx   !< Number of nodes in x direction.
03927   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           Ny   !< Number of nodes in y direction.
03928   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           Nz   !< Number of nodes in z direction.
03929   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           X0   !< X coordinate of origin.
03930   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           Y0   !< Y coordinate of origin.
03931   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           Z0   !< Z coordinate of origin.
03932   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           Dx   !< Space step in x direction.
03933   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           Dy   !< Space step in y direction.
03934   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           Dz   !< Space step in z direction.
03935   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf   !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
03936   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
03937   integer(I4P)::                       rf   !< Real file index.
03938   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03939 
03940   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03941   E_IO = -1_I4P
03942   rf = f
03943   if (present(cf)) then
03944     rf = cf ; f = cf
03945   endif
03946   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
03947   case(ascii)
03948     write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)'DIMENSIONS '//trim(str(.true.,Nx))//' '//trim(str(.true.,Ny))//' '//trim(str(.true.,Nz))
03949     write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)'ORIGIN '//trim(str(n=X0))//' '//trim(str(n=Y0))//' '//trim(str(n=Z0))
03950     write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)'SPACING '//trim(str(n=Dx))//' '//trim(str(n=Dy))//' '//trim(str(n=Dz))
03951   case(raw)
03952     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'DIMENSIONS '//trim(str(.true.,Nx))//' '//trim(str(.true.,Ny))//' '//trim(str(.true.,Nz))//end_rec
03953     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'ORIGIN '//trim(str(n=X0))//' '//trim(str(n=Y0))//' '//trim(str(n=Z0))//end_rec
03954     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'SPACING '//trim(str(n=Dx))//' '//trim(str(n=Dy))//' '//trim(str(n=Dz))//end_rec
03955   endselect
03956   return
03957   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03958   endfunction VTK_GEO_STRP_R8
03959 
03962   function VTK_GEO_STRP_R4(Nx,Ny,Nz,X0,Y0,Z0,Dx,Dy,Dz,cf) result(E_IO)
03963   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03964   implicit none
03965   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           Nx   !< Number of nodes in x direction.
03966   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           Ny   !< Number of nodes in y direction.
03967   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           Nz   !< Number of nodes in z direction.
03968   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::           X0   !< X coordinate of origin.
03969   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::           Y0   !< Y coordinate of origin.
03970   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::           Z0   !< Z coordinate of origin.
03971   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::           Dx   !< Space step in x direction.
03972   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::           Dy   !< Space step in y direction.
03973   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::           Dz   !< Space step in z direction.
03974   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf   !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
03975   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
03976   integer(I4P)::                       rf   !< Real file index.
03977   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03978 
03979   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
03980   E_IO = -1_I4P
03981   rf = f
03982   if (present(cf)) then
03983     rf = cf ; f = cf
03984   endif
03985   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
03986   case(ascii)
03987     write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)'DIMENSIONS '//trim(str(.true.,Nx))//' '//trim(str(.true.,Ny))//' '//trim(str(.true.,Nz))
03988     write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)'ORIGIN '//trim(str(n=X0))//' '//trim(str(n=Y0))//' '//trim(str(n=Z0))
03989     write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)'SPACING '//trim(str(n=Dx))//' '//trim(str(n=Dy))//' '//trim(str(n=Dz))
03990   case(raw)
03991     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'DIMENSIONS '//trim(str(.true.,Nx))//' '//trim(str(.true.,Ny))//' '//trim(str(.true.,Nz))//end_rec
03992     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'ORIGIN '//trim(str(n=X0))//' '//trim(str(n=Y0))//' '//trim(str(n=Z0))//end_rec
03993     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'SPACING '//trim(str(n=Dx))//' '//trim(str(n=Dy))//' '//trim(str(n=Dz))//end_rec
03994   endselect
03995   return

04089   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           Y(1:,1:,1:) !< Y coordinates [1:Nx,1:Ny,1:Nz].

04091   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf          !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).

04337   function VTK_GEO_RECT_R8(Nx,Ny,Nz,X,Y,Z,cf) result(E_IO)
04338   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04339   implicit none
04340   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           Nx       !< Number of nodes in x direction.
04341   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           Ny       !< Number of nodes in y direction.
04342   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           Nz       !< Number of nodes in z direction.
04343   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           X(1:Nx)  !< X coordinates.
04344   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           Y(1:Ny)  !< Y coordinates.
04345   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           Z(1:Nz)  !< Z coordinates.
04346   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf       !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
04347   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO     !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
04348   integer(I4P)::                       rf       !< Real file index.
04349   integer(I4P)::                       n1       !< Counter.
04350   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04351 
04352   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04353   E_IO = -1_I4P
04354   rf = f
04355   if (present(cf)) then
04356     rf = cf ; f = cf
04357   endif
04358   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
04359   case(ascii)
04360     write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)'DIMENSIONS '//trim(str(.true.,Nx))//' '//trim(str(.true.,Ny))//' '//trim(str(.true.,Nz))
04361     write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)'X_COORDINATES '//trim(str(.true.,Nx))//' double'
04362     do n1=1,Nx
04363       write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)str(n=X(n1))
04364     enddo
04365     write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)'Y_COORDINATES '//trim(str(.true.,Ny))//' double'
04366     do n1=1,Ny
04367       write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)str(n=Y(n1))
04368     enddo
04369     write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)'Z_COORDINATES '//trim(str(.true.,Nz))//' double'
04370     do n1=1,Nz
04371       write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)str(n=Z(n1))
04372     enddo
04373   case(raw)
04374     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'DIMENSIONS '//trim(str(.true.,Nx))//' '//trim(str(.true.,Ny))//' '//trim(str(.true.,Nz))//end_rec
04375     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'X_COORDINATES '//trim(str(.true.,Nx))//' double'//end_rec
04376     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)X
04377     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)end_rec
04378     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'Y_COORDINATES '//trim(str(.true.,Ny))//' double'//end_rec
04379     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)Y
04380     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)end_rec
04381     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'Z_COORDINATES '//trim(str(.true.,Nz))//' double'//end_rec
04382     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)Z
04383     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)end_rec
04384   endselect
04385   return
04386   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04387   endfunction VTK_GEO_RECT_R8
04388

04395   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           Ny       !< Number of nodes in y direction.

04397   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::           X(1:Nx)  !< X coordinates.
04398   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::           Y(1:Ny)  !< Y coordinates.
04399   real(R4P),    intent(IN)::           Z(1:Nz)  !< Z coordinates.
04400   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf       !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
04401   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO     !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
04402   integer(I4P)::                       rf       !< Real file index.
04403   integer(I4P)::                       n1       !< Counter.
04404   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04405 
04406   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04407   E_IO = -1_I4P
04408   rf = f
04409   if (present(cf)) then
04410     rf = cf ; f = cf
04411   endif
04412   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
04413   case(ascii)
04414     write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)'DIMENSIONS '//trim(str(.true.,Nx))//' '//trim(str(.true.,Ny))//' '//trim(str(.true.,Nz))
04415     write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)'X_COORDINATES '//trim(str(.true.,Nx))//' float'

04417       write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)str(n=X(n1))
04418     enddo
04419     write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)'Y_COORDINATES '//trim(str(.true.,Ny))//' float'

04421       write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)str(n=Y(n1))
04422     enddo
04423     write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)'Z_COORDINATES '//trim(str(.true.,Nz))//' float'
04424     do n1=1,Nz
04425       write(vtk(rf)%u,'(A)',iostat=E_IO)str(n=Z(n1))
04426     enddo
04427   case(raw)
04428     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'DIMENSIONS '//trim(str(.true.,Nx))//' '//trim(str(.true.,Ny))//' '//trim(str(.true.,Nz))//end_rec
04429     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'X_COORDINATES '//trim(str(.true.,Nx))//' float'//end_rec
04430     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)X
04431     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)end_rec
04432     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'Y_COORDINATES '//trim(str(.true.,Ny))//' float'//end_rec
04433     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)Y
04434     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)end_rec
04435     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'Z_COORDINATES '//trim(str(.true.,Nz))//' float'//end_rec
04436     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)Z
04437     write(vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)end_rec
04438   endselect
04439   return

04445   function VTK_GEO_UNST_R8(NN,X,Y,Z,cf) result(E_IO)
04446   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04447   implicit none
04448   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NN       !< Number of nodes.
04449   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           X(1:)    !< X coordinates of all nodes [1:NN].
04450   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           Y(1:)    !< Y coordinates of all nodes [1:NN].
04451   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           Z(1:)    !< Z coordinates of all nodes [1:NN].
04452   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf       !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
04453   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO     !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
04454   integer(I4P)::                       rf       !< Real file index.
04455   integer(I4P)::                       n1       !< Counter.
04456   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04457 
04458   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04459   E_IO = -1_I4P
04460   rf = f
04461   if (present(cf)) then
04462     rf = cf ; f = cf
04463   endif
04464   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
04465   case(ascii)
04466     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)'POINTS '//str(.true.,NN)//' double'
04467     do n1=1,NN
04468       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)str(n=X(n1))//' '//str(n=Y(n1))//' '//str(n=Z(n1))
04469     enddo
04470   case(raw)
04471     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'POINTS '//str(.true.,NN)//' double'//end_rec
04472     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)(X(n1),Y(n1),Z(n1),n1=1,NN)
04473     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)end_rec
04474   endselect
04475   return
04476   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04477   endfunction VTK_GEO_UNST_R8

04623   function VTK_CON(NC,connect,cell_type,cf) result(E_IO)
04624   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04625   implicit none
04626   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NC              !< Number of cells.
04627   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           connect(:)      !< Mesh connectivity.
04628   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           cell_type(1:NC) !< VTK cell type.
04629   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf              !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
04630   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO            !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
04631   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer        !< Buffer string.
04632   integer(I4P)::                       ncon            !< Dimension of connectivity vector.
04633   integer(I4P)::                       rf              !< Real file index.
04634   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04635 
04636   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04637   E_IO = -1_I4P
04638   rf = f
04639   if (present(cf)) then
04640     rf = cf ; f = cf
04641   endif
04642   ncon = size(connect,1)
04643   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
04644   case(ascii)
04645     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A,2'//FI4P//')',iostat=E_IO)'CELLS ',NC,ncon
04646     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt=FI4P,             iostat=E_IO)connect
04647     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A,'//FI4P//')', iostat=E_IO)'CELL_TYPES ',NC
04648     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt=FI4P,             iostat=E_IO)cell_type
04649   case(raw)
04650     write(s_buffer,      fmt='(A,2'//FI4P//')',iostat=E_IO)'CELLS ',NC,ncon
04651     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,                      iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
04652     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,                      iostat=E_IO)connect
04653     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,                      iostat=E_IO)end_rec
04654     write(s_buffer,      fmt='(A,'//FI4P//')', iostat=E_IO)'CELL_TYPES ',NC
04655     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,                      iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
04656     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,                      iostat=E_IO)cell_type
04657     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,                      iostat=E_IO)end_rec
04658   endselect
04659   return
04660   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04661   endfunction VTK_CON
04662 
04678   function VTK_DAT(NC_NN,var_location,cf) result(E_IO)
04679   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04680   implicit none
04681   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NC_NN        !< Number of cells or nodes of field.
04682   character(*), intent(IN)::           var_location !< Location of saving variables: cell for cell-centered, node for node-centered.
04683   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf           !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
04684   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO         !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
04685   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer     !< Buffer string.
04686   integer(I4P)::                       rf           !< Real file index.
04687   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04688 
04689   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04690   E_IO = -1_I4P
04691   rf = f
04692   if (present(cf)) then
04693     rf = cf ; f = cf
04694   endif
04695   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
04696   case(ascii)
04697     select case(trim(Upper_Case(var_location)))
04698     case('CELL')
04699       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A,'//FI4P//')',iostat=E_IO)'CELL_DATA ',NC_NN
04700     case('NODE')
04701       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A,'//FI4P//')',iostat=E_IO)'POINT_DATA ',NC_NN
04702     endselect
04703   case(raw)
04704     select case(trim(Upper_Case(var_location)))
04705     case('CELL')
04706       write(s_buffer,fmt='(A,'//FI4P//')',iostat=E_IO)'CELL_DATA ',NC_NN
04707       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
04708     case('NODE')
04709       write(s_buffer,fmt='(A,'//FI4P//')',iostat=E_IO)'POINT_DATA ',NC_NN
04710       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
04711     endselect
04712   endselect
04713   return
04714   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04715   endfunction VTK_DAT
04716 
04721   function VTK_VAR_SCAL_R8(NC_NN,varname,var,cf) result(E_IO)
04722   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04723   implicit none
04724   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NC_NN        !< Number of nodes or cells.
04725   character(*), intent(IN)::           varname      !< Variable name.
04726   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           var(1:NC_NN) !< Variable to be saved.
04727   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf           !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
04728   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO         !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
04729   integer(I4P)::                       rf           !< Real file index.
04730   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04731 
04732   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04733   E_IO = -1_I4P
04734   rf = f
04735   if (present(cf)) then
04736     rf = cf ; f = cf
04737   endif
04738   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
04739   case(ascii)
04740     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)'SCALARS '//trim(varname)//' double 1'
04741     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)'LOOKUP_TABLE default'
04742     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt=FR8P, iostat=E_IO)var
04743   case(raw)
04744     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'SCALARS '//trim(varname)//' double 1'//end_rec
04745     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)'LOOKUP_TABLE default'//end_rec
04746     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)var
04747     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)end_rec
04748   endselect
04749   return
04750   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04751   endfunction VTK_VAR_SCAL_R8

04816   endselect

04824   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04825   implicit none
04826   character(*), intent(IN)::           vec_type      !< Vector type: vect = generic vector , norm = normal vector.
04827   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NC_NN         !< Number of nodes or cells.
04828   character(*), intent(IN)::           varname       !< Variable name.
04829   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           varX(1:NC_NN) !< X component of vector.
04830   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           varY(1:NC_NN) !< Y component of vector.
04831   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           varZ(1:NC_NN) !< Z component of vector.
04832   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf            !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
04833   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO          !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
04834   integer(I4P)::                       rf            !< Real file index.
04835   integer(I8P)::                       n1            !< Counter.

04837 
04838   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04839   E_IO = -1_I4P
04840   rf = f
04841   if (present(cf)) then
04842     rf = cf ; f = cf
04843   endif
04844   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
04845   case(ascii)
04846     select case(Upper_Case(trim(vec_type)))
04847     case('VECT')
04848       write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A)',iostat=E_IO)'VECTORS '//trim(varname)//' double'

04851     endselect

04853   case(raw)

04857     case('NORM')

04859     endselect

04950   function VTK_VAR_TEXT_R8(NC_NN,dimm,varname,textCoo,cf) result(E_IO)
04951   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04952   implicit none
04953   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           NC_NN                   !< Number of nodes or cells.
04954   integer(I4P), intent(IN)::           dimm                    !< Texture dimensions.
04955   character(*), intent(IN)::           varname                 !< Variable name.
04956   real(R8P),    intent(IN)::           textCoo(1:NC_NN,1:dimm) !< Texture.
04957   integer(I4P), intent(IN), optional:: cf                      !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
04958   integer(I4P)::                       E_IO              !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
04959   character(len=maxlen)::              s_buffer                !< Buffer string.
04960   integer(I4P)::                       rf                      !< Real file index.
04961   integer(I8P)::                       n1,n2                   !< Counters.
04962   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04963 
04964   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04965   E_IO = -1_I4P
04966   rf = f
04967   if (present(cf)) then
04968     rf = cf ; f = cf
04969   endif
04970   select case(vtk(rf)%f)
04971   case(ascii)
04972     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt='(A,1X,'//FI4P//',1X,A)',iostat=E_IO)'TEXTURE_COORDINATES '//trim(varname),dimm,' double'
04973     write(s_buffer,fmt='(I1)',iostat=E_IO)dimm
04974     s_buffer='('//trim(s_buffer)//FR4P//')'
04975     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,fmt=trim(s_buffer),iostat=E_IO)((textCoo(n1,n2),n2=1,dimm),n1=1,NC_NN)
04976   case(raw)
04977     write(s_buffer,fmt='(A,1X,'//FI4P//',1X,A)',iostat=E_IO)'TEXTURE_COORDINATES '//trim(varname),dimm,' double'
04978     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)trim(s_buffer)//end_rec
04979     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)((textCoo(n1,n2),n2=1,dimm),n1=1,NC_NN)
04980     write(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)end_rec
04981   endselect
04982   return
04983   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
04984   endfunction VTK_VAR_TEXT_R8

05037   function VTK_END(cf) result(E_IO)
05038   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
05039   implicit none
05040   integer(I4P), intent(INOUT), optional:: cf   !< Current file index (for concurrent files IO).
05041   integer(I4P)::                          E_IO !< Input/Output inquiring flag: $0$ if IO is done, $> 0$ if IO is not done.
05042   integer(I4P)::                          rf   !< Real file index.
05043   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
05044 
05045   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
05046   E_IO = -1_I4P
05047   rf = f
05048   if (present(cf)) then
05049     rf = cf ; f = cf
05050   endif
05051   close(unit=vtk(rf)%u,iostat=E_IO)
05052   call vtk_update(act='remove',cf=rf,Nvtk=Nvtk,vtk=vtk)
05053   f = rf
05054   if (present(cf)) cf = rf
05055   return
05056   !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
05057   endfunction VTK_END
05058 endmodule Lib_VTK_IO
